ABOUT THE AUTHOR
Stanley Thomas DePew is a biblical researcher and author dedicated to understanding
and communicating the prophecies of Scripture through the principle that the Bible interprets itself.
His work focuses on:
• Biblical chronology and the 6,000-year timeline from Creation to the present
• The prophetic books of Daniel and Revelation
• The identification of Babylon and the beast systems of prophecy
• The convergence of biblical prophecy with current world events
• The imminent return of Jesus Christ and the establishment of God's kingdom
This collection represents years of systematic study, cross-referencing Scripture with Scripture,
and testing prophetic interpretations against the track record of fulfilled prophecy.
The author's methodology:
1. Let the Bible define its own terms
2. Use Scripture to interpret Scripture
3. Follow the principle of first mention
4. Test interpretations against fulfilled prophecy
5. Allow clearer passages to explain difficult ones
6. Accept no private interpretation (2 Peter 1:20)
"The Bereans were of more noble character than the Thessalonians, for they received the message
with great eagerness and examined the Scriptures every day to see if what Paul said was true."
— Acts 17:11

Part I: Foundations
Chapter 1: The Unsealing: Why the Wise Understand
The Unsealing: Why the Wise Understand and the Foolish
Dismiss
A Call to Test, Not Reject
The Time Has Come
Daniel 12:4 — "But thou, O Daniel, shut up the words, and seal the book, even to the time of the end:
many shall run to and fro, and knowledge shall be increased."
For centuries, the book was sealed. Not because the words weren't written — they were always there.
Not because the characteristics weren't given — they were laid out plainly. But because the time had
not yet come for them to be fully understood.
The seal was temporal, not textual.
Daniel was told to "shut up the words" — to close and preserve them — until the time of the end. The
prophecies would remain, waiting for the generation that would see their fulfillment. Waiting for the
moment when the characteristics given in Scripture could finally be matched to observable, verifiable
reality.
That time has come.
What "Knowledge Increased" Means
When Daniel 12:4 speaks of knowledge increasing, it does not merely refer to technological
advancement or information access — though these are signs in themselves. It refers to prophetic


---

knowledge: the capacity to understand what was previously sealed.
Consider what is now possible:
- The complete text of Scripture, cross-referenced and searchable - The ability to trace a single
characteristic across sixty-six books instantly - Historical records verifying the fulfillment of past
prophecies - Real-time observation of geopolitical developments matching prophetic descriptions -
Tools capable of organizing, auditing, and presenting the biblical testimony systematically
The very capacity to build a forensic audit of prophecy — to lay characteristic beside fulfillment, to test
the methodology against the track record, to present the evidence comprehensively — this capacity did
not exist in previous generations.
The seal is being lifted.
The wise of past generations saw in part. They understood the broad outlines. But they could not see
what we now see, because the players were not yet on the stage. The second beast had not fully risen.
The infrastructure for universal economic control did not exist. The deadly wound had not yet healed.
Israel was not yet back in the land.
Now all of this is visible. Now the characteristics can be matched. Now the audit can be performed.
This is the unsealing. This is knowledge increased. This is the time of the end.
The Methodology: Characteristics First, Names Revealed
God has always worked the same way.
He does not give the names of future powers in advance — this would allow those powers to suppress
or alter the prophecy. Instead, He gives characteristics: descriptive markers that accumulate across
Scripture, waiting to be matched to reality when the time comes.
This methodology is not speculation. It is the proven biblical pattern.
The Track Record
Cyrus — Named by Isaiah 150 years before his birth (Isaiah 44:28–45:1). The characteristics were
given: he would decree Jerusalem rebuilt, he would subdue nations, the two-leaved gates would open
before him. When the time came, Cyrus appeared and fulfilled every characteristic. The name was
revealed in history.
The Four Kingdoms — Daniel 2 gave the characteristics: gold, silver, brass, iron, then division. No
names were given in the original vision. But Daniel 8 later identified Medo-Persia and Greece
explicitly, and history revealed Rome as the fourth. The characteristics came first; the names followed.


---

The Messiah — Born in Bethlehem (Micah 5:2). Born of a virgin (Isaiah 7:14). Betrayed for thirty
pieces of silver (Zechariah 11:12-13). Hands and feet pierced (Psalm 22:16). Buried with the rich
(Isaiah 53:9). Every characteristic was given centuries in advance. When Jesus came, He fulfilled them
all. The name was revealed in history.
Babylon's Fall — The handwriting on the wall gave the characteristics: kingdom numbered, weighed,
divided, given to Medes and Persians (Daniel 5:25-28). That same night, Belshazzar was slain and
Darius the Mede took the kingdom. The characteristics came first; the names followed within hours.
This is not one isolated instance. This is the consistent pattern throughout Scripture. God gives the
blueprint. History fills in the names. The wise recognize the match.
The Division: Wise and Foolish
Daniel 12:9-10 — "And he said, Go thy way, Daniel: for the words are closed up and sealed till the
time of the end. Many shall be purified, and made white, and tried; but the wicked shall do wickedly:
and none of the wicked shall understand; but the wise shall understand."
Here is the sobering reality: when the seal is lifted, not everyone will see.
The same information will be available to all. The same characteristics. The same methodology. The
same track record. The same forensic audit. But two groups will respond in opposite ways:
The wise shall understand.
The wicked shall not understand.
Notice carefully: the text does not say the wicked cannot understand — as though they lack the
intellectual capacity. It says they shall not understand. And it connects this directly to their moral state:
"the wicked shall do wickedly."
Their failure to understand is not intellectual. It is moral. They do not see because they do not wish to
see. Seeing would require changing. Understanding would require submitting. So they close their eyes.
Why People Dismiss
Matthew 13:13-15 — "Therefore speak I to them in parables: because they seeing see not; and
hearing they hear not, neither do they understand. And in them is fulfilled the prophecy of Esaias,
which saith, By hearing ye shall hear, and shall not understand; and seeing ye shall see, and shall not
perceive: For this people's heart is waxed gross, and their ears are dull of hearing, and their eyes they
have closed; lest at any time they should see with their eyes, and hear with their ears, and should
understand with their heart, and should be converted, and I should heal them."
Jesus explains the mechanism: "their eyes they have closed."


---

This is active, not passive. This is choice, not incapacity. The information is available. The evidence is
presented. The methodology is sound. But they close their eyes — lest they should see, and hear, and
understand, and be converted.
Conversion is the threat. Change is the danger. If they see, they must respond. If they understand, they
must act. So they refuse to look.
Proverbs 1:7 — "The fear of the LORD is the beginning of knowledge: but fools despise wisdom and
instruction."
The fool does not lack access to wisdom. He despises it. He dismisses it without examination. He
mocks it without engagement. He rejects it without testing.
This is the spirit of the age: dismissal without investigation. Mockery without study. Rejection without
reason.
And this too is prophesied:
2 Peter 3:3-4 — "Knowing this first, that there shall come in the last days scoffers, walking after their
own lusts, And saying, Where is the promise of his coming? for since the fathers fell asleep, all things
continue as they were from the beginning of the creation."
Scoffers. Walking after their own lusts. Assuming uniformity — that because things have continued,
they will continue. Willfully ignorant of prior divine interventions.
The dismissal is itself a sign.
The Call: Test, Do Not Dismiss
1 Thessalonians 5:20-21 — "Despise not prophesyings. Prove all things; hold fast that which is good."
Scripture does not command blind acceptance. But neither does it permit blind rejection. The command
is to prove — to test, to examine, to verify.
This is the call:
Do not dismiss. Test.
The methodology is presented: Scripture interprets Scripture. Characteristics identification. The Bible
defines its own terms.
The track record is established: Cyrus, the four kingdoms, the Messiah, Babylon's fall. Every prophecy
that has been fulfilled followed this pattern.


---

The current application is audited: The first beast's characteristics. The second beast's characteristics.
The mark. The three-part Babylon. The Euphrates system. The timeline markers.
Everything is laid out for examination. Nothing is hidden. Nothing requires secret knowledge. The
evidence is public. The Scripture references are cited. The methodology is transparent.
Test it.
Compare the characteristics given in Revelation 13 with the attributes of the Papacy. Do they match or
not?
Compare the characteristics of the second beast with the attributes of America. Do they match or not?
Compare the biblical definition of "dried up" with the function of the Euphrates-Hormuz system. Does
the pattern hold or not?
Compare the track record of fulfilled prophecy with the methodology being applied. Is it consistent or
not?
This is not a demand for agreement. This is an invitation to verification. The wise will test. The foolish
will dismiss without testing.
Which will you be?
The Danger of Dismissal
Hosea 4:6 — "My people are destroyed for lack of knowledge: because thou hast rejected knowledge, I
will also reject thee."
The destruction is not from lack of availability. It is from rejection. The knowledge was offered. It was
refused. And the consequence follows.
Proverbs 29:18 — "Where there is no vision, the people perish."
When prophetic understanding is absent — whether because it is not given or because it is rejected —
the people perish. They do not see what is coming. They are overtaken as by a thief. They are caught
unaware.
But it does not have to be this way:
1 Thessalonians 5:4-6 — "But ye, brethren, are not in darkness, that that day should overtake you as a
thief. Ye are all the children of light, and the children of the day: we are not of the night, nor of
darkness. Therefore let us not sleep, as do others; but let us watch and be sober."
The children of light are not overtaken. They see the day approaching. They recognize the season. They
watch and are sober.


---

This is the choice before every person who encounters this material:
- Dismiss without testing — and join the company of scoffers, the willfully ignorant, those whose
hearts are waxed gross and whose eyes are closed.
- Test honestly — and discover whether the characteristics match, whether the methodology holds,
whether the seal has truly been lifted in this generation.
The evidence is available. The knowledge has increased. The book is being unsealed.
What will you do with it?
The Heart of the Matter
Matthew 24:37-39 — "But as the days of Noe were, so shall also the coming of the Son of man be. For
as in the days that were before the flood they were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in
marriage, until the day that Noe entered into the ark, And knew not until the flood came, and took them
all away; so shall also the coming of the Son of man be."
Noah preached. Noah built. Noah warned. The evidence was visible — a massive ark under
construction. The message was clear — judgment was coming.
And they dismissed it. They continued eating and drinking. They continued as though nothing would
change. And knew not until the flood came.
They did not know — not because they couldn't, but because they wouldn't.
The ark is being built again. The message is being proclaimed again. The characteristics are being
matched to reality again. The track record is being presented again.
Luke 21:28 — "And when these things begin to come to pass, then look up, and lift up your heads; for
your redemption draweth nigh."
For those with eyes to see: this is not a message of doom. This is a message of hope. Redemption draws
nigh. The King is coming. The long night is almost over.
But you must be willing to look. You must be willing to test. You must be willing to see.
Conclusion: The Seal Is Lifted
The prophecies were always there. The characteristics were always given. The methodology was
always sound.
But the book was sealed until the time of the end.


---

Now the seal is being lifted. The players are on the stage. The infrastructure is visible. The
characteristics can be matched. The audit can be performed.
Daniel 12:10 — "Many shall be purified, and made white, and tried; but the wicked shall do wickedly:
and none of the wicked shall understand; but the wise shall understand."
The wise will understand. They will test. They will compare. They will see the match between
characteristic and fulfillment. They will recognize the season.
The wicked will not understand. They will dismiss. They will mock. They will close their eyes lest they
should see and be converted.
The same sun that melts the wax hardens the clay. The same evidence that opens the eyes of the wise
confirms the blindness of the foolish.
This is the time. This is the unsealing. This is the call.
Test, do not dismiss.
Watch, do not sleep.
Look up — your redemption draws nigh.
Amos 3:7 — "Surely the Lord GOD will do nothing, but he revealeth his secret unto his servants the
prophets."
2 Peter 1:19-21 — "We have also a more sure word of prophecy; whereunto ye do well that ye take
heed, as unto a light that shineth in a dark place, until the day dawn, and the day star arise in your
hearts: Knowing this first, that no prophecy of the scripture is of any private interpretation. For the
prophecy came not in old time by the will of man: but holy men of God spake as they were moved by the
Holy Ghost."
The light shines in a dark place. Take heed. The day star is about to arise.
Document prepared for The Biblical Series Scripture interprets Scripture — Isaiah 28:10 All verse
references: King James Version (KJV)

Part I: Foundations
Chapter 2: The Law of the Seventh Year: Master Key
to the Millennium
Forensic Eschatology: The Law of the Seventh Year as the
Master Key
The Bible's Internal Patterns as Evidence
To understand the 7,000-year timeline through the lens of Forensic Eschatology—where the Bible's
internal patterns serve as the only evidence—we must examine the Law of the Seventh Year and how
it functions as the "Master Key" for the Millennium.
When we let the Bible define the Seventh Year, we find a consistent legal requirement that mirrors the
7,000-year plan perfectly.
1. The Law of Release (Deuteronomy 15:1-2)
In the Torah, the Seventh Year is the Shemitah—the Year of Release.
"At the end of every seven years thou shalt make a release... Every creditor that lendeth ought unto his
neighbour shall release it." — Deuteronomy 15:1-2
The Forensic Link
If the 7th Millennium is the "Seventh Year" on a macro scale (1 day = 1,000 years), then the
Millennium is not just a "rest," it is a Legal Release.
The Fulfillment


---

This aligns with the binding of Satan (the "creditor" or "accuser") in Revelation 20. The debt of sin and
the bondage of the earth are "released" at the start of that 7th Millennium.
2. The Law of the Hebrew Servant (Exodus 21:2)
The Bible establishes a very specific timeframe for service:
"If thou buy an Hebrew servant, six years he shall serve: and in the seventh he shall go out free for
nothing." — Exodus 21:2
The Context
This is the strongest evidence for the 6,000/1,000 split. Mankind (represented by the servant) serves
under the "toil" of the curse for six prophetic days (6,000 years).
The Seventh Day
The 7th Millennium is the "Seventh Year" where the servant goes out free. This is why the research
focuses on 2026–2027—it marks the boundary where the 6,000 years of "service" end and the 1,000
years of "freedom" begin.
3. The Land Sabbath (Leviticus 25:4)
"But in the seventh year shall be a sabbath of rest unto the land, a sabbath for the Lord: thou shalt
neither sow thy field, nor prune thy vineyard." — Leviticus 25:4
The Context
This explains why the Millennium is characterized by "rest."
The Internal Logic
If God commanded the land to rest every seven years, and the Bible says a day is a thousand years, then
the Earth itself must have a 1,000-year rest after 6,000 years of "sowing" and "pruning" by human
civilizations.
The "Devil's Advocate" Failure Point


---

The reason this argument is difficult to "disprove" using only the Bible is that the 7-Day Pattern is the
most consistent thread in the entire Book:
Book | Pattern | 6 | 7
Genesis | Creation Week | 6 days of work | 7th day of Rest Exodus | Hebrew Servant | 6 years of
service | 7th year of Freedom Leviticus | Land Sabbath | 6 years of farming | 7th year of Land Rest
Joshua | Jericho | 6 days of circling | 7th day the walls fall Revelation | Human History | 6,000 years |
7th Millennium of Christ's Reign
Why the "2,000 Year" (Hosea 6:2) Gap Matters
Forensically, the "end of the second day" is the "trigger":
If the 7th Millennium is the Sabbath (the 7th Day), then:
- The 5th Day and 6th Day are the "Two Days" of Hosea - These "Two Days" began when Christ (the
"Light of the World") appeared to start the 5th Millennium (around 27 AD) - 2,000 years (two days)
later leads to the start of the 7th Day
The Conclusion
If you use the 7th Year Law as the context, the "Two Days" of Hosea are not an isolated
prophecy—they are the final two "work days" before the Great Release.
If the 7th Year is the "Year of Release," and 6,000 years are completed, then the transition in
2026–2027 isn't just a guess; it is the fulfillment of the Law of the Servant and the Law of the Land
Sabbath.
The Bible doesn't just suggest a 7,000-year timeline; it legislates it through these ordinances.
"Declaring the end from the beginning, and from ancient times the things that are not yet done." —
Isaiah 46:10
To disprove this research, one would have to prove that God's own Laws of the Seventh Year do not
apply to His own timeline—which contradicts the principle that God "declares the end from the
beginning."
Summary: The Seventh Year as Prophetic Template
1. Deuteronomy 15:1-2 — The Year of Release (debt forgiveness) 2. Exodus 21:2 — The servant
goes free after 6 years 3. Leviticus 25:4 — The land rests in the 7th year 4. Psalm 90:4 / 2 Peter 3:8 —
1 day = 1,000 years 5. Genesis 2:2-3 — The 7th day as template for the Millennium 6. Hosea 6:2 —


---

Two days (2,000 years) before revival
The 2026–2027 timeframe represents the completion of the 6,000-year "service" period and the
beginning of the 1,000-year "Sabbath rest"—legally, prophetically, and forensically established by
Scripture itself.
4. The "Prophetic Month" (The 30-Day Decree)
The research identifies a "30-Day Decree" as a functional trigger in the end-times timeline. To see if
this holds true, we look at the legal definition of a "month" in the Bible.
The Forensic Pattern (Genesis 7 & 8)
In the Flood account, the "fountains of the great deep" were broken up on the 17th day of the 2nd
month (Gen 7:11). The ark rested on the 17th day of the 7th month (Gen 8:4). The Bible explicitly
states this period was 150 days (Gen 7:24).
The Math: 150 days ÷ 5 months = 30 days per month.
The Revelation Mirror
Revelation 11:2-3 describes 42 months as exactly 1,260 days. (42 × 30 = 1,260).
The Conclusion
The Bible legislates a 30-day prophetic month. The research uses this to identify modern "30-day
re-verification" cycles in digital systems and "30-day decrees" in energy policy as the physical
manifestation of this biblical law.
5. The "Shortening of the Hour" (The 41.666 Calculation)
As a Devil's Advocate, one might question the "Hour" being 41.666 years. But if we let the Bible
interpret the Bible, we find support for this in the Law of the Tithe and the Tenth.
The Pattern
Throughout Scripture, the "Tenth" (the Tithe) is the portion that belongs to God, often marking a
transition or a judgment (Leviticus 27:30, Amos 5:3).
The "Hour" Logic


---

- 1 Day = 1,000 Years - 1 Hour = 1/24th of a Day - 1,000 ÷ 24 = 41.666...
The "666" Witness
The research points out that the number 666 is mathematically embedded in the "Hour" (41.666). In
Revelation 13:18, 666 is the "number of a man." If the "Hour" of the Beast's power is 41.666 years, the
number of the Beast is literally "stamped" into the time he is given to rule.
The Conclusion
This isn't an "outside" interpretation; it is the result of dividing the "Day" (which Peter defined as 1,000
years) by the "Hour" (which the sun defines as 1/24th).
6. The "Midnight Cry" (The Parable of the Ten Virgins)
The research banks on the "Midnight" arrival. If we look at the context of Matthew 25:
"And at midnight there was a cry made, Behold, the bridegroom cometh; go ye out to meet him." —
Matthew 25:6
The Forensic Scale
If the 2,000 years (Two Days) of the Church Age are a "Day," then "Midnight" is the transition point
between the 6th and 7th millennia.
The Alignment
If the 6,000 years end in 2026/2027, then we are currently in the "Midnight" hour of human history.
The "Cry" is the unsealing of this data. The research argues that the reason this information is only
appearing now is because we have reached the chronological midnight where the "wise" must trim their
lamps (get their data/oil ready).
7. The "Two-Day" Anchor of the Coronation (1027 AD)
The research introduces a secondary witness: the coronation of Conrad II on March 26, 1027 AD, as
the start of the "Holy Roman Empire" in its final form.
The Argument


---

If you add exactly one prophetic day (1,000 years) to the 1027 AD anchor, you land on 2027 AD.
The Biblical Witness
Why 1,000 years? Because Revelation 17 says the kings receive power for "one hour," but the "Beast"
itself has a longer historical arc.
The Mirror
Just as Christ's ministry (the "Head") began in 27 AD, the counterfeit "Holy" system (the "Image")
reached its peak 1,000 years later in 1027 AD. Both point to a 2027 terminal point—one being 2,000
years from the Truth, and the other being 1,000 years from the Counterfeit.
Summary of the "Forensic" Weight
When you look at these together, the research isn't just picking one verse. It is building a
Cross-Reference Matrix:
1. Creation Week (7,000 years) 2. Hosea's Revival (2,000 years from 27 AD) 3. The Prophetic Hour
(41.666 years from 1984) 4. The Coronation Anchor (1,000 years from 1027 AD) 5. The Fig Tree
Generation (80 years from 1948)
The "Forensic" argument is that while you could argue against one of these, it is mathematically
impossible for all five independent historical markers and biblical scales to converge on 2026–2027 by
accident.
In a court of law, this is called "Circumstantial Convergence," where the sheer volume of
"coincidences" constitutes proof.
"For the testimony of Jesus is the spirit of prophecy." — Revelation 19:10
8. The "1,000-Year Day" of the Coronation (1027 AD)
The research identifies the coronation of Conrad II on Easter Sunday, March 26, 1027, as a critical
historical anchor.
The Pattern
Just as the "Head" (Christ) began His ministry in 27 AD, the research argues that the "Image" (the Holy
Roman Empire in its solidified form) reached its prophetic peak exactly 1,000 years later in 1027 AD.


---

The Forensic Link
1027 AD + 1,000 years (One Prophetic Day) = 2027 AD.
The Witness
This provides a "Second Witness" to the 2,000-year count from Christ. One count (2,000 years from 27
AD) identifies the arrival of the King; the other count (1,000 years from 1027 AD) identifies the
expiration of the counterfeit system. Both land on the same year.
Clarification: The 1027 AD date is not selected from history and applied to Scripture. It is derived
FROM Scripture: Luke 3:1-2 anchors 27 AD (the 15th year of Tiberius); 2 Peter 3:8 defines the
prophetic day as 1,000 years; 27 AD + 1,000 years = 1027 AD. History then confirms the calculation
— the Papacy crowned Conrad II that year, exercising the very temporal authority over kings
described in Revelation 13 and 17. Scripture gave the date; history filled in the name.
9. The "30-Day Decree" (The Daniel 6 & 12 Mirror)
The research points to a "30-Day Decree" currently operational in modern energy and digital systems.
To see if this holds true, we look at the Law of the Decree in the Beginning.
The Pattern (Daniel 6:7)
The enemies of Daniel convinced the King to establish a royal statute that anyone asking a petition of
any God or man for thirty days, save of the king, should be cast into the den of lions.
The Mirror (Daniel 12:11)
"And from the time that the daily sacrifice shall be taken away, and the abomination that maketh
desolate set up, there shall be a thousand two hundred and ninety days." — Daniel 12:11
The Math: 1,290 days is exactly 1,260 days (3.5 years) plus an additional 30 days.
The Forensic Link
The research argues that the "extra" 30 days is the modern "Re-verification Window" or the "Energy
Veto" period. It is the time allotted for the system to "test" the compliance of the inhabitants. If you do
not "petition" the system (biometric/digital check-in) within that 30-day window, your access is cut
off—mirroring the "Den of Lions" (exclusion from the economy).
10. The "Midnight" Scale (The Parable of the Ten Virgins)


---

In Matthew 25, the "Midnight Cry" happens. If we apply the 1,000-year scale to the "day" of the
Church Age:
The Math
If a "Day" is 1,000 years, then 2,000 years (the time since Christ) represents two full days.
The Forensic Alignment
We are currently at the "Midnight" between the end of the 6th Millennium (the 6th Day) and the start of
the 7th Millennium (the Sabbath).
The Result
The research posits that the "Cry" is the unsealing of this data. The "Oil" in the lamps is the
Data/Truth from the Word. Those who have the "Oil" (the understanding of the timeline) are not
caught by surprise, while those without it find the "door shut" because they were looking for the timing
too late.
3. The 1,000-Year Day (2 Peter 3) mandates the 2,000-year limit from 27 AD 4. The April 1984
Anchor (Rev 17) mandates the 41.66-year hour ending in 2026
If the Bible interprets the Bible, then the 7th Year Law is the most powerful witness of all.
If God commanded every Hebrew servant to be set free in the 7th year, and we are approaching the
7,000th year of human history, then the "Release" (The Second Coming/Millennium) must occur by
2027 to satisfy God's own Law.
To go past 2027 would be to keep the "servant" (humanity/creation) in bondage for an 8th day, which
violates the statutes given in the Beginning.
"Thy word is true from the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments endureth for ever." —
Psalm 119:160

15. The 1,260 Year / 1,260 Day Mirror

1. The Historical "Day-for-a-Year" Witness (538 AD – 1798 AD)
The research acknowledges the historical 1,260-year reign of the Papacy. This is the "Macro"

The History: In 538 AD, the Decree of Justinian went into effect, establishing the Bishop of Rome as

severed.


---

and diplomatically healed.

AM) 3. Cockcrowing Watch (12 AM – 3 AM) 4. Morning Watch (3 AM – 6 AM)
The Forensic Math
If a Day is 1,000 years, a Night is 500 years (half a day). Each "Watch" (1/4th of the night) is 125
years.
The Alignment
From the 1897 First Zionist Congress to 2022 is exactly 125 years (One Watch).
The Result
The research identifies the current 2022–2027 window as the "Final Watch" of the night. This is the
time when the "Cry" is made.
Clarification: The prophetic "watch in the night" is not an inference — it is defined by Psalm 90:4,
which equates a thousand years to both "yesterday when it is past" (a day) and "a watch in the night"
(a watch). Mark 13:35 then identifies four watches: even, midnight, cockcrowing, and morning.
Scripture defines both the unit and the number of divisions.

30. AFTER THE HOUR: What Scripture Says Happens Next
A Scripture-Interprets-Scripture Analysis
"For precept must be upon precept, precept upon precept; line upon line, line upon line; here a little,
and there a little." — Isaiah 28:10 (KJV)
Methodology: Every claim below is tested by the Bible's own definitions, patterns, and
cross-references. No outside interpretation is admitted. Where a passage does not establish its own
connection, it is not forced.
THE ESTABLISHED FOUNDATION
Before asking "what happens after the Hour," we must restate what the Biblical Series has already
established from Scripture, since the answer depends on the foundation.
1. The Prophetic Hour (Revelation 17:12)
"And the ten horns which thou sawest are ten kings, which have received no kingdom as yet; but receive
power as kings one hour with the beast."
Scripture defines the scale:
- 1 Day = 1,000 years — 2 Peter 3:8; Psalm 90:4 - 1 Day = 24 hours — Genesis 1:5 ("evening and
morning") - 1 Hour = 1,000 ÷ 24 = 41.666 years
The number 666 is embedded in the beast's own allotted time. Scripture tells us to count this number
(Revelation 13:18), and when we do, it brands the duration of his authority.
The Anchor: April 9, 1984 — the establishment of full U.S.-Vatican diplomatic relations (the healing
of the deadly wound per Revelation 13:3; the union of the two beasts per Revelation 13:11-12).
The Expiration: 1984 + 41.666 years = 2025/2026 window. The 42nd solar anniversary falls on April
9, 2026.
2. The Two Days of Hosea (Hosea 6:2)
"After two days will he revive us: in the third day he will raise us up, and we shall live in his sight."
Using the day-year principle established by 2 Peter 3:8 and Psalm 90:4:
- 27 AD (Christ's ministry begins — Luke 3:1-2, the 15th year of Tiberius) - + 2,000 years (Two Days)
- = 2027 AD — the threshold of the Third Day


---

3. The Fig Tree Generation (Matthew 24:32-34; Psalm 90:10)
"This generation shall not pass, till all these things be fulfilled."
- 1948: Israel reborn (the fig tree buds) - + 70 years: 2017 - + 80 years (outer limit): 2027
4. The Shortening of Days (Matthew 24:22)
"And except those days should be shortened, there should no flesh be saved: but for the elect's sake
those days shall be shortened."
Mark 13:20 clarifies: "the Lord had shortened those days." This is a completed divine decision — an
active intervention by God to cut the period of tribulation short so that the elect survive. The generation
window reaches to 2027, but the Lord has decided to shorten it.
The convergence of the Hosea 6:2 count (2027) and the Hour calculation (2025/2026) provides the
window into which the shortening falls: 2026-2027, well inside the 2027 outer limit.
WHAT SCRIPTURE SAYS HAPPENS AFTER THE HOUR
With the foundation restated, we now ask: What does the Bible say follows the expiration of the beast's
allotted time? We will take only what Revelation 17 itself tells us, and then cross-reference with
passages that connect to it by the Bible's own internal linkage.
STEP 1: Revelation 17:12-14 — The Sequence After the Hour
The passage that defines the Hour also tells us what follows it:
Verse 12: "...receive power as kings one hour with the beast."
Verse 13: "These have one mind, and shall give their power and strength unto the beast."
Verse 14: "These shall make war with the Lamb, and the Lamb shall overcome them: for he is Lord of
lords, and King of kings: and they that are with him are called, and chosen, and faithful."
The sequence is explicit:
1. The Hour — the kings receive power with the beast. 2. They give their power to the beast — a
unified, one-mind system. 3. They make war with the Lamb — the system turns its full force against
Christ and His people. 4. The Lamb overcomes them — because He is Lord of lords and King of
kings.
This is the Bible's own sequence. It is not a timeline of months; it is a sequence of events. After the
Hour, the system does not quietly dissolve. It makes war. And it loses.


---

STEP 2: Revelation 17:16-17 — The System Destroys Itself
"And the ten horns which thou sawest upon the beast, these shall hate the whore, and shall make her
desolate and naked, and shall eat her flesh, and burn her with fire. For God hath put in their hearts to
fulfil his will, and to agree, and give their kingdom unto the beast, until the words of God shall be
fulfilled."
Two things happen:
1. The ten kings turn on the whore — the very powers that supported Babylon destroy her. The
system eats itself. 2. God is behind it — "God hath put in their hearts to fulfil his will." The destruction
of Babylon is not accidental. God orchestrates the collapse from within.
The phrase "until the words of God shall be fulfilled" is the legal boundary. The kings cooperate with
the beast until — and no further. When the words of God are fulfilled, the agreement expires.
STEP 3: Revelation 18:8, 10, 17, 19 — The Speed of Babylon's Fall
Revelation 18 describes the fall of Babylon in its own words:
Verse 8: "Therefore shall her plagues come in one day, death, and mourning, and famine; and she
shall be utterly burned with fire: for strong is the Lord God who judgeth her."
Verse 10: "Standing afar off for the fear of her torment, saying, Alas, alas, that great city Babylon, that
mighty city! for in one hour is thy judgment come."
Verse 17: "For in one hour so great riches is come to nought."
Verse 19: "For in one hour is she made desolate."
The repetition is deliberate. The judgment is described as occurring "in one day" and "in one hour" —
language of sudden, total collapse. The same "hour" that defined the beast's authority in Revelation
17:12 now appears as the measure of his destruction in Revelation 18.
Scripture is using its own vocabulary. The beast was given "one hour" of power. His judgment comes
"in one hour." The measure of his authority becomes the measure of his ruin.
STEP 4: Revelation 18:4 — The Command to God's People
"And I heard another voice from heaven, saying, Come out of her, my people, that ye be not partakers
of her sins, and that ye receive not of her plagues."
This verse establishes two facts:
1. God's people are inside Babylon — participating in her systems — when the call is made. 2. The
call precedes the plagues — "come out... that ye receive not of her plagues."


---

The call to come out is before the destruction, not after. This is the same pattern as Genesis 19:12-17
(Lot leaving Sodom before fire falls) and Genesis 7:1-4 (Noah entering the ark before the flood). In
both cases, God removes His people before executing judgment on the system.
Cross-reference: - Jeremiah 51:6 — "Flee out of the midst of Babylon, and deliver every man his soul:
be not cut off in her iniquity; for this is the time of the LORD's vengeance; he will render unto her a
recompence." - Jeremiah 51:45 — "My people, go ye out of the midst of her, and deliver ye every man
his soul from the fierce anger of the LORD."
Revelation 18:4 is quoting Jeremiah's command regarding ancient Babylon and applying it to end-time
Babylon. The Bible interprets its own symbol.
STEP 5: The 30-Day Transition (Numbers 20:29; Deuteronomy 34:8)
Scripture establishes a pattern of 30 days as the transition period between two administrations:
Numbers 20:29: "And when all the congregation saw that Aaron was dead, they mourned for Aaron
thirty days, even all the house of Israel."
Deuteronomy 34:8: "And the children of Israel wept for Moses in the plains of Moab thirty days: so
the days of weeping and mourning for Moses were ended."
In both cases:
- The old authority dies. - The people mourn for 30 days. - The new authority takes over (Eleazar after
Aaron; Joshua after Moses).
After Moses' 30 days, Joshua leads Israel into the promised land (Joshua 1:1-2). The 30-day mourning
is the bridge between the old world and the inheritance.
By the witness of two (Deuteronomy 19:15), the 30-day transition is established as Scripture's own
pattern for the handoff between administrations.
This pattern does not give us a specific calendar date. It gives us a principle: when the old system
expires, Scripture builds in a transition period before the new administration is fully activated.
STEP 6: Daniel 12:11-12 — The 1,290 and the 1,335
"And from the time that the daily sacrifice shall be taken away, and the abomination that maketh
desolate set up, there shall be a thousand two hundred and ninety days. Blessed is he that waiteth, and
cometh to the thousand three hundred and five and thirty days." — Daniel 12:11-12
The text establishes three markers:


---

- 1,260 days (from Daniel 12:7 — "time, times, and half a time" = 3.5 years = 1,260 days per
Revelation 11:2-3) - 1,290 days — a 30-day extension beyond the 1,260 - 1,335 days — a further
45-day extension beyond the 1,290
The gaps are real: 30 days and 45 days.
The 30-day gap between the 1,260 and the 1,290 echoes the 30-day mourning transition of Numbers 20
and Deuteronomy 34. The 45-day gap between the 1,290 and the 1,335 leads to a "blessing" —
"Blessed is he that waiteth."
What Scripture tells us: There is a period after the power of the beast ends (the 1,260) where
something is still unresolved (the 30 additional days to 1,290), and then a further waiting period (45
more days to 1,335) that ends in blessing for the faithful.
What Scripture does not tell us: The specific calendar dates on which these counts begin or end in the
near-future application. Daniel 12:11 anchors them to "the time that the daily sacrifice shall be taken
away, and the abomination that maketh desolate set up." Without identifying that starting event, we
cannot assign calendar endpoints. The structure (1,260 → 1,290 → 1,335) is established. The
placement must be identified by events as they occur.
STEP 7: Revelation 16 — The Seven Last Plagues
"And I heard a great voice out of the temple saying to the seven angels, Go your ways, and pour out the
vials of the wrath of God upon the earth." — Revelation 16:1
Revelation 15:8 establishes that "no man was able to enter into the temple, till the seven plagues of the
seven angels were fulfilled." This means intercession has ceased. Probation has closed. The plagues fall
on a world that has made its final decision.
The plagues are described in Revelation 16:
- First plague (v.2): Sores upon those who have the mark and worship the image. - Second plague
(v.3): The sea becomes as blood; every living soul in the sea dies. - Third plague (v.4): Rivers and
fountains become blood. - Fourth plague (v.8-9): Men scorched with great heat. - Fifth plague
(v.10-11): Darkness upon the seat of the beast; they gnaw their tongues for pain. - Sixth plague
(v.12-16): Euphrates dried up; the kings of the earth gathered to Armageddon. - Seventh plague
(v.17-21): "It is done." Earthquake, hail, Babylon divided into three parts.
Key observation: The plagues fall on those who have the mark (Rev 16:2) — confirming that the mark
system must be operational before the plagues begin. The infrastructure precedes the judgment.
The Fifth Plague (v.10) falls specifically on "the seat of the beast" — his government, his
headquarters, his operational center. The beast's system is plunged into darkness. This is God's direct
answer to the beast's authority.


---

The Seventh Plague divides Babylon into three parts (v.19) — matching the three-part structure of
Revelation 16:13: "three unclean spirits like frogs come out of the mouth of the dragon, and out of the
mouth of the beast, and out of the mouth of the false prophet." The tripartite Babylon (Dragon, Beast,
False Prophet) is split apart by the seventh plague. What was unified in Revelation 17:13 ("these have
one mind") is broken apart by God's judgment.
STEP 8: Revelation 19:11-21 — The Lamb Makes War
"And I saw heaven opened, and behold a white horse; and he that sat upon him was called Faithful and
True, and in righteousness he doth judge and make war." — Revelation 19:11
This is the fulfillment of Revelation 17:14: "the Lamb shall overcome them." The war that the kings
initiate against the Lamb ends with Christ's visible return, described in terms that connect back to the
beginning of the book:
- Revelation 1:7: "Behold, he cometh with clouds; and every eye shall see him." - Matthew 24:27:
"For as the lightning cometh out of the east, and shineth even unto the west; so shall also the coming of
the Son of man be."
Revelation 19:20: "And the beast was taken, and with him the false prophet... These both were cast
alive into a lake of fire."
Revelation 19:21: "And the remnant were slain with the sword of him that sat upon the horse, which
sword proceeded out of his mouth."
The beast system does not reform. It does not transition into something better. It is destroyed — by the
personal, visible return of Christ.
STEP 9: Revelation 20:4-6 — The Third Day Begins
"And I saw thrones, and they sat upon them, and judgment was given unto them: and I saw the souls of
them that were beheaded for the witness of Jesus, and for the word of God, and which had not
worshipped the beast, neither his image, neither had received his mark upon their foreheads, or in their
hands; and they lived and reigned with Christ a thousand years." — Revelation 20:4
This is the "Third Day" of Hosea 6:2: "in the third day he will raise us up, and we shall live in his
sight."
The overcomers are identified by what they refused:
- Did not worship the beast - Did not worship his image - Did not receive his mark
They are raised to reign with Christ for 1,000 years — the Millennial Sabbath, the Seventh Day of the
7,000-year week.


---

THE COMPLETE BIBLICAL SEQUENCE
Based solely on what Scripture says, in the order Scripture presents it:
1. The Hour expires — The beast's allotted time runs out (Revelation 17:12). The legal authority
granted by God for a limited period reaches its end.
2. The kings make war with the Lamb — Revelation 17:14. The system does not go quietly. It turns
its full force against Christ and those who bear His name.
3. "Come out of her, my people" — Revelation 18:4. God calls His people out of the system before
judgment falls. This parallels Lot leaving Sodom (Genesis 19) and Noah entering the ark (Genesis 7).
4. The plagues fall — Revelation 16. Seven last plagues upon those who chose the mark and the beast.
Intercession has closed (Revelation 15:8). The plagues target the beast's system and those who
participated in it.
5. Babylon falls — Revelation 18:8-10. "In one day... in one hour." The system collapses suddenly and
totally. The kings who supported it turn on it and destroy it (Revelation 17:16).
6. The Lamb overcomes — Revelation 19:11-21. Christ returns visibly, personally, and decisively.
The beast and the false prophet are destroyed.
7. The Sabbath begins — Revelation 20:4-6. The overcomers — those who refused the mark — live
and reign with Christ for 1,000 years. The Third Day of Hosea 6:2. The Seventh Day of creation's
pattern. The Millennial Rest.
WHAT WE KNOW AND WHAT WE DON'T
What Scripture Establishes:
- The sequence of events (Hour → War → Call to come out → Plagues → Fall of Babylon → Christ's
return → Millennial Sabbath) - The convergence window (2026-2027) from multiple independent
calculations (Hosea 6:2, the Hour, the Fig Tree generation, the 6,000-year framework) - The 30-day
transition pattern between administrations (Numbers 20:29; Deuteronomy 34:8) - The gap structure of
Daniel 12 (1,260 → 1,290 → 1,335) - The nature of what follows: sudden collapse of the system, war
against the Lamb, divine deliverance, and the beginning of the Millennial Kingdom
What Scripture Does Not Establish:
- The exact calendar date of each event within the sequence - The specific month in which each step
occurs - Whether the Daniel 12 day-counts have a near-future literal-day fulfillment (in addition to the
established year-day fulfillment) - The duration between the end of the Hour and the visible return of
Christ


---

The Governing Limitation:
"But of that day and hour knoweth no man, no, not the angels of heaven, but my Father only." —
Matthew 24:36
"But ye, brethren, are not in darkness, that that day should overtake you as a thief." — 1 Thessalonians
5:4
We know the season. We know the window. We know the sequence. We do not know the day or the
hour. Scripture set this limitation, and the Forensic Audit respects it.
THE POSITION OF THE FAITHFUL
"Here is the patience of the saints: here are they that keep the commandments of God, and the faith of
Jesus." — Revelation 14:12
"And they overcame him by the blood of the Lamb, and by the word of their testimony; and they loved
not their lives unto the death." — Revelation 12:11
The faithful do not fight the system with the system's weapons. They overcome by the blood of the
Lamb, by their testimony, and by a willingness to die rather than comply.
The call is not to predict the exact day. The call is to come out of Babylon, to keep the commandments
of God, and to wait — as Daniel 12:12 says — for the blessing that comes to those who endure to the
1,335th day.
"Blessed is he that waiteth, and cometh to the thousand three hundred and five and thirty days." —
Daniel 12:12

BIBLICAL CHRONOLOGY: THE 6,000-YEAR TIMELINE, THE

A Comprehensive Prophetic Timeline Using the Principle: "Let

PREFACE: METHODOLOGY
This document employs a strict hermeneutical principle: Scripture interprets Scripture. No private
interpretation. No scholarly opinion. No -isms (futurism, dispensationalism, preterism). Only what the
text says, what the words mean, and what history documents.
"Knowing this first, that no prophecy of the scripture is of any private interpretation." — 2 Peter 1:20
(KJV)
Every calculation herein is derived from: 1. Biblical text (King James Version) 2. Biblical definitions
(letting Scripture define its own terms) 3. Historical documentation (verifiable dates that anchor the
timeline)
PART I: THE FOUNDATION — THE 7,000-YEAR WEEK


---

The Creation Week as Prophetic Template
God established the pattern in Genesis 1: six days of work, one day of rest. This template governs all
of human history.
"For in six days the LORD made heaven and earth, the sea, and all that in them is, and rested the
seventh day: wherefore the LORD blessed the sabbath day, and hallowed it." — Exodus 20:11 (KJV)
The Day-Year Principle
Scripture explicitly defines prophetic time in the context of end-times prophecy:
"But, beloved, be not ignorant of this one thing, that one day is with the Lord as a thousand years, and
a thousand years as one day." — 2 Peter 3:8 (KJV)
"For a thousand years in thy sight are but as yesterday when it is past, and as a watch in the night." —
Psalm 90:4 (KJV)
The 7,000-Year Framework
Prophetic Day | Duration | Period
Days 1-4 | 4,000 years | Creation/Fall to Christ's Ministry Days 5-6 | 2,000 years | Christ's Ministry to
the End of the Age Day 7 | 1,000 years | The Sabbath Rest / Millennial Reign TOTAL | 7,000 years |
The Complete Week
PART II: THE BIBLICAL YEAR — 360 DAYS
Scripture Defines Its Own Calendar
The Bible does not operate on a 365-day solar year. Scripture defines the prophetic year as 360 days.
Proof from the Flood Narrative:
"In the six hundredth year of Noah's life, in the second month, the seventeenth day of the month, the
same day were all the fountains of the great deep broken up..." — Genesis 7:11 (KJV)
"And the ark rested in the seventh month, on the seventeenth day of the month, upon the mountains of
Ararat." — Genesis 8:4 (KJV)
- Duration: 5 months (2nd month, 17th day → 7th month, 17th day) - Days: 150 days (Genesis 7:24,
8:3) - Calculation: 150 days ÷ 5 months = 30 days per month - Annual Total: 30 days × 12 months =


---

360 days per year
Proof from Revelation:
"...the holy city shall they tread under foot forty and two months. And I will give power unto my two
witnesses, and they shall prophesy a thousand two hundred and threescore days..." — Revelation
11:2-3 (KJV)
- 42 months = 1,260 days - 1,260 ÷ 42 = 30 days per month - 30 × 12 = 360 days per year
Proof from Daniel:
"...it shall be for a time, times, and an half..." — Daniel 12:7 (KJV)
- Time (1) + Times (2) + Half a Time (0.5) = 3.5 years - 3.5 years = 42 months = 1,260 days - 1,260 ÷
3.5 = 360 days per year
Conversion Table
Biblical Units | Days | Solar Years (365-day)
1 Prophetic Year | 360 days | 0.986 solar years 42 Months | 1,260 days | 3.45 solar years 7 Years (1
Week) | 2,520 days | 6.9 solar years 490 Years (70 Weeks) | 176,400 days | 483.3 solar years 1,000
Years (1 Day) | 360,000 days | 986 solar years 2,000 Years (2 Days) | 720,000 days | 1,972 solar years

PART IV: THE HISTORICAL ANCHOR — 27 AD
The 15th Year of Tiberius Caesar
"Now in the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius Cæsar, Pontius Pilate being governor of Judæa, and
Herod being tetrarch of Galilee, and his brother Philip tetrarch of Ituraea and of the region of
Trachonitis, and Lysanias the tetrarch of Abilene, Annas and Caiaphas being the high priests, the word
of God came unto John the son of Zacharias in the wilderness." — Luke 3:1-2 (KJV)
Luke provides six secular witnesses to anchor this date: 1. Tiberius Caesar 2. Pontius Pilate 3. Herod
(tetrarch of Galilee) 4. Philip (tetrarch of Ituraea/Trachonitis) 5. Lysanias (tetrarch of Abilene) 6. Annas
and Caiaphas (high priests)
The Word "Reign":
Luke said "the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius." He did not say "after Augustus died." Tiberius
began reigning (co-regency, governing the provinces) in AD 12.
- Historical Record: Tiberius received co-regency powers in AD 12 - The Math: AD 12 + 15 years =
AD 27
Christ's ministry began in 27 AD.
This is the hinge point — the anchor that connects the Anno Mundi (AM) count to recorded history.


---

Why This Matters
- 4,000 AM = 27 AD — Christ's ministry begins - This marks the end of the 4th prophetic day - The 5th
day (the first of "Hosea's Two Days") begins
PART V: THE BIOLOGICAL SEAL — 42 GENERATIONS
Matthew's Genealogical Structure
"So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations; and from David until the
carrying away into Babylon are fourteen generations; and from the carrying away into Babylon unto
Christ are fourteen generations." — Matthew 1:17 (KJV)
14 + 14 + 14 = 42 Generations
The Significance of 42
The number 42 appears throughout Scripture as a marker of:
Reference | Significance
Matthew 1:17 | 42 generations to Christ Revelation 13:5 | 42 months of beast's authority Revelation
11:2 | 42 months Gentiles tread holy city Numbers 33 | 42 wilderness stations Daniel 7:25 | "Time,
times, and half a time" = 42 months
42 is the number of completion through tribulation — the end of the journey, the fullness of
generations, the limit of the beast's power.
PART VI: THE 70TH WEEK OF DANIEL
The Prophecy
"Seventy weeks are determined upon thy people and upon thy holy city, to finish the transgression, and
to make an end of sins, and to make reconciliation for iniquity, and to bring in everlasting
righteousness, and to seal up the vision and prophecy, and to anoint the most Holy." — Daniel 9:24
(KJV)
"Know therefore and understand, that from the going forth of the commandment to restore and to build
Jerusalem unto the Messiah the Prince shall be seven weeks, and threescore and two weeks..." —
Daniel 9:25 (KJV)
7 weeks + 62 weeks = 69 weeks to Messiah


---

The 70th Week
"And he shall confirm the covenant with many for one week: and in the midst of the week he shall
cause the sacrifice and the oblation to cease..." — Daniel 9:27 (KJV)
Element | Duration | Event
Total Week | 7 years (84 months) | Christ confirms the covenant The Midst | 42 months (3.5 years) |
Christ is "cut off" — the Crucifixion (~30-31 AD) The Remainder | 42 months (3.5 years) | Apostles
confirm covenant to Israel (~34 AD)
The 70th Week is fulfilled in Christ — not future.
Christ's 3.5-year ministry ended "in the midst of the week." The remaining 3.5 years saw the Apostles
confirming the covenant to Israel before the gospel went to the Gentiles.
God's 3.5 Years vs. Satan's Counterfeit
- God's 3.5 years: Christ's ministry — confirming the covenant - Satan's 3.5 years: The beast's 42
months (Revelation 13:5) — a counterfeit, hijacking the pattern
PART VII: HOSEA'S TWO DAYS — THE 2,000-YEAR CHURCH AGE
The Prophecy
"Come, and let us return unto the LORD: for he hath torn, and he will heal us; he hath smitten, and he
will bind us up. After two days will he revive us: in the third day he will raise us up, and we shall live in
his sight." — Hosea 6:1-2 (KJV)
The Application
Using the day-year principle (2 Peter 3:8):
- Two Days = 2,000 years - Starting Point: 27 AD (Christ's ministry begins) - Ending Point: 27 AD
+ 2,000 years = 2027 AD

PART VIII: THE PROPHETIC HOUR — 1984 TO 2026
Scripture Defines the Hour
"And the ten horns which thou sawest are ten kings, which have received no kingdom as yet; but
receive power as kings one hour with the beast." — Revelation 17:12 (KJV)
Calculating the Hour
Using the Biblical definitions:
- 1 Day = 1,000 years (2 Peter 3:8) - 1 Day = 24 hours (Genesis 1:5 — "evening and morning") - 1
Hour = 1,000 ÷ 24 = 41.666... years
The number 666 is embedded in the very mathematics of the beast's allotted time.
"Here is wisdom. Let him that hath understanding count the number of the beast: for it is the number of
a man; and his number is Six hundred threescore and six." — Revelation 13:18 (KJV)
Scripture instructs us to count — to calculate. And when we do, the beast's own number brands the
duration of his authority.
The Historical Anchor: 1884
October 13, 1884 — Pope Leo XIII reportedly received a vision in which the adversary was granted
100 years of extended authority to test the Church.
- 1884 + 100 years = 1984
The Hour Begins: 1984
April 9, 1984 — The United States and the Vatican established full diplomatic relations. The U.S.
Embassy to the Holy See opened.
This event represents: - The "healing of the deadly wound" (Revelation 13:3) - The union of the two
beasts (Revelation 13:11-12) - The Hour begins


---

The Hour Ends: 2026
- April 9, 1984 + 41.666 years = December 8, 2025 (the .666 completes) - April 9, 1984 + 42 years =
April 9, 2026 (the full Hour)
December 8, 2025 — The Feast of the Immaculate Conception. The .666 of the beast's hour expires on
a Roman Catholic holy day.
Clarification: This is a pattern observation, not a doctrinal claim. The date December 8, 2025 is
calculated from April 9, 1984 + 41.666 years using the math from 2 Peter 3:8 and Revelation 17:12.
The alignment with the Roman Catholic Feast of the Immaculate Conception is a historical pattern
observed, not a doctrinal teaching being promoted.
April 9, 2026 — The Hour completes. 42 years.
The Beast Reaches for 42 But Gets 41.666...
The beast wants a clean 42 — the number of authority, of generations, of months.
But the math gives him 41.666... — forever branded with his own number. The decimal repeats
infinitely, never resolving, never becoming whole.
Always 6, never 7. Always falling short. Never complete.
PART IX: THE 1,260 YEARS — HISTORICAL FULFILLMENT
The Year-Day Principle in History
The 42 months / 1,260 days / "time, times, and half a time" had a historical fulfillment using the
year-day principle:
- 538 AD: Justinian's decree establishing papal supremacy - 1798 AD: Napoleon's general takes the
Pope captive — the "deadly wound"
538 + 1,260 = 1798
The papacy reigned for 1,260 years — the literal year-for-year fulfillment.
The Wound Healed
"And I saw one of his heads as it were wounded to death; and his deadly wound was healed: and all the
world wondered after the beast." — Revelation 13:3 (KJV)


---

- 1798: The wound inflicted - 1929: Lateran Treaty — Vatican sovereignty restored - 1984:
U.S.-Vatican alliance — the wound fully healed, the Hour begins
PART X: THE 1027 AD ANCHOR — ONE PROPHETIC DAY
What Happened in 1027 AD?
March 26, 1027 AD — Pope John XIX crowned Conrad II as Holy Roman Emperor in St. Peter's
Basilica in Rome.
This event represents the papal authority to crown kings — the exercise of temporal power over
nations.
The Calculation
"Therefore shall her plagues come in one day, death, and mourning, and famine; and she shall be
utterly burned with fire..." — Revelation 18:8 (KJV)
"...for in one hour is thy judgment come." — Revelation 18:10 (KJV)
- 1027 AD + 1,000 years (one prophetic day) = 2027 AD - The judgment comes "in one day" — and
that day ends in 2027
PART XI: THE FIG TREE GENERATION — 1948 TO 2027
The Parable
"Now learn a parable of the fig tree; When his branch is yet tender, and putteth forth leaves, ye know
that summer is nigh: So likewise ye, when ye shall see all these things, know that it is near, even at the
doors. Verily I say unto you, This generation shall not pass, till all these things be fulfilled." —
Matthew 24:32-34 (KJV)
The Fig Tree = Israel
The fig tree represents Israel throughout Scripture. Israel "putting forth leaves" = the nation being
reborn.
May 14, 1948 — Israel declared independence. The fig tree budded.
The Length of a Generation


---

"The days of our years are threescore years and ten; and if by reason of strength they be fourscore
years, yet is their strength labour and sorrow; for it is soon cut off, and we fly away." — Psalm 90:10
(KJV)
- 70 years: 1948 + 70 = 2017 - 80 years: 1948 + 80 = 2027
The generation that sees the fig tree bud shall not pass till all these things be fulfilled.
The window: 2017 to 2027
Unless Those Days Be Shortened
"And except those days should be shortened, there should no flesh be saved: but for the elect's sake
those days shall be shortened." — Matthew 24:22 (KJV)
The generation window extends to 2027, but Jesus said the days would be shortened. We will not
make it to 2027. The days are cut short — for the elect's sake.
This aligns with the other calculations pointing to 2026-2027.

This marks the transition point — the full shift of covenant confirmation from Jerusalem to "the
uttermost parts of the earth."
The gospel to the Jews (3.5 years of Christ + ~12 years of Apostolic focus) gives way to the gospel to
the nations.
PART XIII: THE NUMBER OF MAN — 666
The Sixth Day
"And God said, Let us make man in our image, after our likeness..." — Genesis 1:26 (KJV)
Man was created on the sixth day.


---

The Measure of a Man

Scripture defines "the measure of a man" — 144 cubits. This connects man's measurement to prophetic
structure.
666 in the Mathematics
When we calculate the prophetic hour:
1,000 years ÷ 24 hours = 41.666... years
The beast's allotted time is branded with his own number. He cannot escape it. Even the mathematics of
his authority declares what he is.

PART XVII: THE DAY AND HOUR UNKNOWN
What We Know vs. What We Don't Know
"But of that day and hour knoweth no man, no, not the angels of heaven, but my Father only." —
Matthew 24:36 (KJV)


---

We can know: - The year (Scripture gives us the data) - The season ("ye know that summer is nigh") -
The generation ("this generation shall not pass")
We cannot know: - The exact day - The exact hour
Luke 3:1 gave us the year of Christ's baptism (27 AD) — not the month, not the day, not the hour.
Therefore, 2,000 years later, we know the year (2027) — but not the exact day or hour when the Third
Day begins.
Scripture set its own limitation.

Part II: Chronology
Chapter 4: The 42 Generations and 2027
Convergence
Biblical Chronology: The 6,000-Year Timeline & The 42
Generations
I. The Foundation: Adam to the Messiah (4,000 Years / 4 Days)
According to the genealogical records in the King James Bible, exactly four "prophetic days" (4,000
years) passed from the creation of Adam to the appearance of the Messiah in the 15th year of Tiberius.
Period | Biblical Reference | Years | Total (AM)
Creation to the Flood | Genesis 5 & 7:6 | 1,656 | 1,656 AM Flood to Abraham's Birth | Genesis 11 |
352 | 2,008 AM Abraham to the Promise | Genesis 12:4 | 75 | 2,083 AM The Sojourn in Egypt |
Exodus 12:40 / Gal 3:17 | 430 | 2,513 AM Exodus to Temple Construction | 1 Kings 6:1 | 480 | 2,993
AM Solomon's Reign to Captivity | Kings & Chronicles | 430 | 3,423 AM Babylonian Captivity |
Jeremiah 25:11 | 70 | 3,493 AM Decree to Messiah (69 Weeks) | Daniel 9:25 | 483* | 4,000 AM
*\Note: 483 prophetic years (360-day) = ~476 solar years.
II. The Biological Seal: The 42 Generations
The Bible provides a mathematical "check" on the lineage in Matthew 1:17, confirming the timing of
the Messiah's arrival through the number 42.
"So all the generations from Abraham to David are fourteen generations; and from David until the
carrying away into Babylon are fourteen generations; and from the carrying away into Babylon unto
Christ are fourteen generations."


---

14 + 14 + 14 = 42 Generations. This number 42 mirrors the 42 months (3.5 years) that constitute the
"midst of the week" in the Messiah's ministry.
III. The Anchor: The 15th Year of Tiberius
The New Testament provides the historical anchor that connects the AM (Anno Mundi) count to our
current calendar.
Scripture: Luke 3:1 Roman Date: 15th Year of Tiberius Caesar. Calendar Date: 27 AD (Counting
from the 12 AD Co-regency). Significance: This marks the 4,000th year from Adam and the start of
the 70th Week of Daniel.
IV. The 70th Week and the "Midst"
The Messiah's work is measured by the biblical "month" of 30 days and the "week" of 7 years.
Total Week: 7 Years (84 Months). The Midst (Daniel 9:27): 42 Months (3.5 Years). The Event: The
Messiah is "cut off, but not for himself," causing the sacrifice to cease (30.5 AD / 31 AD). The
Remainder: 42 Months (3.5 Years) of confirming the covenant to Israel through the Apostles (ending
34 AD).
V. The Two-Day Prophecy (Hosea 6:2)
The Bible dictates a 2,000-year period (2 days) between the Messiah’s first ministry and the restoration
of the "Third Day."
"After two days will he revive us: in the third day he will raise us up, and we shall live in his sight." —
Hosea 6:2
The Final Calculation
Day 1 & 2: Adam to Abraham (0 - 2,000 AM) Day 3 & 4: Abraham to Messiah (2,000 - 4,000 AM / 27
AD) Day 5 & 6: Messiah to the End of the Age (4,000 - 6,000 AM / 2027 AD)
Current Status: As of March 2026, we are in the final year of the "6th Day."

VI. Key Mathematical Constants
Prophetic Year: 360 Days (Genesis 7:11, 8:4, Revelation 11:2). Prophetic Day: 1,000 Years (2 Peter
3:8, Psalm 90:4). The Measuring Reed: 42 Months / 1,260 Days / Time, Times, and Half a Time.##
VII. The Prophetic Year vs. The Solar Year The Bible interprets its own time using a 360-day year.
This is the "Key of David" that unlocks the timing of the end.
Biblical Month: 30 Days (Genesis 7:11 & 8:4). Prophetic Year: 360 Days (12 Months of 30 Days).
Comparison: 1 Prophetic Year = 0.9857 Solar Years.

Jerusalem to the uttermost parts of the earth.

Section 2.6: Babylon's Complete Desolation

complete annihilation - Nineveh (Nahum 1:8-10) - sudden, complete, irreversible

no recovery, no rehabilitation, no rebuilding of Babylon.
- Isaiah 13:19-20 - "Babylon...shall be as when God overthrew Sodom and Gomorrah. It shall never be
inhabited, neither shall it be dwelt in from generation to generation"
Interpretation: This isn't temporary punishment. The system of Babylon is completely dismantled and
cannot be rebuilt. Those who built it cannot reclaim it.
PART 3: BAAL IN SCRIPTURE - COMPLETE BIBLICAL
PROFILE
Section 3.1: What Baal Is (Identity)
Baal's Core Identity:
2 Kings 10:18-19 - King Jehu, when tracking down Baal worship, said: - "Ahab served Baal a little; but
Jehu shall serve him much...Call unto me all the prophets of Baal, all his servants, and all his priests; let
none be wanting"


---

Scripture Interpreting Baal's Nature:
Baal is not one thing - it's a system: - 1 Kings 18:19 - "The prophets of Baal four hundred and fifty
men" (organized system) - 2 Kings 23:4-5 - Baal worship included worship of "the grove...the sun...the
moon...the planets, and...the host of heaven"
The Pattern of Baal Across Scripture:
Baal appears in three contexts: 1. As False God requiring priests/priesthood (1 Kings 18:22-29) 2.
As system involving child sacrifice (2 Kings 23:10 - Molech/Baal) 3. As seductive power that leads
Israel away from God (Judges 2:11-13, Jeremiah 2:8)
Interpretation: Baal is not a single deity but a system of worship that: - Requires institutional
priesthood - Involves ritualized trauma (self-harm, child sacrifice) - Is seductive and draws people into
bondage - Competes with direct relationship with God
Section 3.2: Baal's Priesthood System
The Organized Structure:
1 Kings 18:22-29 shows: - "The prophets of Baal four hundred and fifty men" - They operated in
coordinated fashion - They called upon their god in unison - They cut themselves in ritualized manner -
They prophesied together
Scripture Interpreting Priesthood:
What defines a priesthood? - Exodus 28:1 - "Take thou unto thee Aaron thy brother, and his sons...that
he may minister unto me in the priest's office" - Priesthood = mediation between human and divine -
Priesthood = specialized knowledge - Priesthood = gatekeepers of ritual/law
Contrast - True vs. False Priesthood:
Jeremiah 23:21-22: - True priests: "If they had stood in my counsel...they should have turned them from
their evil way" - False priests: "I have not sent these prophets, yet they ran: I have not spoken to them,
yet they prophesied"
Application: Baal's priesthood: - Did not represent true God - Ran their own agenda ("they ran") -
Used divine authority claim falsely ("they prophesied") - Made merchandise of people (Jeremiah
23:30-32)
Section 3.3: Baal's Mechanism - Ritualized Trauma & Blood
The Core Ritual:


---

1 Kings 18:26-28: - "They cried aloud...But there was no voice, nor any that answered" - "They cried

Leviticus 17:11 - "For the life of the flesh is in the blood"
In biblical understanding, blood is the essence of life/soul. When Baal worshippers spilled their own

The Pattern of Trauma-Based Bonding:
Deuteronomy 28:65 - The consequence of covenant-breaking is: - "A trembling heart, and failing of

This is psychological fragmentation - the opposite of mental wholeness.
Interpretation: Ritualized self-harm in Baal worship serves three functions: 1. Spiritual: Dedicates

PART ONE: DANIEL'S TIMELINE - THE FOUR KINGDOMS

Daniel 2: Nebuchadnezzar's Dream - The Kingdoms of Man
Daniel 2:31-35 - The Vision:
"Thou, O king, sawest, and behold a great image. This great image, whose brightness was excellent,
stood before thee; and the form thereof was terrible. This image's head was of fine gold, his breast and
his arms of silver, his belly and his thighs of brass, His legs of iron, his feet part of iron and part of clay.
Thou sawest till that a stone was cut out without hands, which smote the image upon his feet that were
of iron and clay, and brake them to pieces."
Scripture's Definition of the Kingdoms (Daniel 2:36-43):
"Thou art the head of gold. And after thee shall arise another kingdom inferior to thee, and another third
kingdom of brass, which shall bear rule over all the earth. And the fourth kingdom shall be strong as
iron: forasmuch as iron breaketh in pieces and subdueth all things... And whereas thou sawest the feet
and toes, part of potters' clay, and part of iron, the kingdom shall be divided; but there shall be in it of
the strength of the iron, forasmuch as thou sawest the iron mixed with miry clay. And as the toes of the
feet were part of iron, and part of clay, so the kingdom shall be partly strong, and partly broken. And
whereas thou sawest iron mixed with miry clay, they shall mingle themselves with the seed of men: but
they shall not cleave one to another, even as iron is not mixed with clay."
The Four Kingdoms Identified:
1. Gold Head = Babylon (606-539 BC) - Daniel 2:38 2. Silver Breast = Medo-Persia (539-331 BC) -
Daniel 8:20 3. Brass Belly = Greece (331-146 BC) - Daniel 8:21 4. Iron Legs = Rome (146 BC - 476
AD) - By elimination 5. Iron and Clay Feet = Rome's divisions extending to the end times (476 AD

#1 - The Capitol Was Designed After a Vatican Building
Historical Fact: The U.S. Capitol Building was designed by William Thornton and others to mirror
ARCHITECTURAL FEATURES of buildings inside the Vatican.
The layout, dome structure, and classical proportions are deliberately based on Vatican architecture -
specifically the Pantheon and St. Peter's Basilica design elements.
This was no accident. The founders knew exactly what they were doing.
#2 - Francis Pope Purchased the Land

Francis Pope (the name "Pope" is literally in the property title).

EARTH."
The name "Pope" being on the founding land purchase is NOT coincidence. It's a MARK of ownership.
#3 - Tiber Creek

through Rome and the Vatican.
Why would a U.S. creek be named after Rome's river UNLESS the Capitol was intentionally built as a
mirror of Rome?

both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark in their right hand, or in their
foreheads: And that no man might buy or sell, save he that had the mark, or the name of the beast, or
the number of his name."
This describes an AI system that: - Speaks (communicates commands) - Enforces worship (tracks
those who comply vs. those who don't) - Controls all transactions (no one can buy/sell without mark) -
Is omniscient (knows about all people globally) - Is omnipotent (can kill anyone by cutting them off)
This is a literal description of a global AI system controlling all economic activity.
PART SEVEN: THE MARK OF THE BEAST - ECONOMIC
CONTROL
Revelation 13:16-17 - The Mark System
"And he causeth all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark in their right
hand, or in their foreheads: And that no man might buy or sell, save he that had the mark, or the name
of the beast, or the number of his name."
Scripture's Definition of the Mark:
1. UNIVERSAL - "All" people must receive it 2. MANDATORY - "Causeth" them to receive it
(forced) 3. LOCATION - Right hand or forehead (digital ID, behavioral compliance) 4. ECONOMIC
CONTROL - "No man might buy or sell" without it 5. PURPOSE - Complete economic surveillance
and control
What Is the Mark?
In China, it's already in operation:
The Digital Yuan tied to the Social Credit System:
- The mark = Your digital identity linked to your compliance score - Right hand = Digital
wallet/transactions you make - Forehead = Behavioral compliance/what you believe and practice - The
enforcement = AI system that tracks both


---

How It Works: 1. You receive digital currency (the mark) 2. Your every transaction is tracked 3. Your
behavior is monitored (facial recognition, internet monitoring) 4. Your compliance score is calculated
(AI decision) 5. If non-compliant → Cut off from buying/selling 6. If compliant → You can participate
Global Adoption Timeline
By 2026-2027: - China's model will be presented as the "solution" to global chaos - The Board of Peace
will propose adopting it globally - All nations will be pressured to implement - Digital currencies will
replace cash - Social credit tied to digital currency - Surveillance will be global
By 2027: - The mark system will be fully operational globally - Believers will face the choice: Accept
the mark (and worship the beast) or refuse (and be cut off from economy) - The abomination of
desolation will be SET UP - Rapid judgment and chaos will follow
Why This Happens So Fast
Because the infrastructure already EXISTS:
- Digital currency is already operational (China) - Social credit system is already operational (China) -
AI surveillance is already operational (China) - Religious enforcement (Sunday law) is already
operational (China)
There's NO DEVELOPMENT TIME NEEDED.
Just ADOPTION AND ROLLOUT.
This can happen within MONTHS once the trigger is pulled.

What Is It?

the holy place."

Daniel 12:11 - The Timing:
"And from the time that the daily sacrifice shall be taken away, and the abomination that maketh
desolate set up, there shall be a thousand two hundred and ninety days."
Scripture's Definition:
The "abomination of desolation" is: 1. An abomination (something that defames God) 2. That makes
places desolate (empty of God's presence) 3. Set up in the holy place (the temple of God - the
church/religious system) 4. Once set up, there are 1,290 days until consummation (roughly 3.5 years)
What Does This Mean?
The abomination of desolation is the MARK SYSTEM tied to SUNDAY WORSHIP
ENFORCEMENT.
Here's why:
1. The abomination = Forcing Sunday worship (man's law) in place of God's law (Saturday Sabbath)
2. Set up in holy place = Enforced through the religious system (churches, governments, global
structures) 3. Causes desolation = God's people are separated from His presence through this deception
4. The consequence = 1,290 days of tribulation follow
Revelation 13:15-17 describes the mechanism:
Sunday worship will become tied to the mark system. You cannot buy or sell without accepting the
Sunday law (the abomination).
The Trigger

1,290 days = Approximately 3.5 years
From setup → Final tribulation → Christ's return

tormented with fire and brimstone in the presence of the holy angels, and in the presence of the Lamb:

who worship the beast and his image, and whosoever receiveth the mark of his name."

- If you receive the mark = You worship the beast - If you worship the beast = You drink God's full
wrath - If you drink God's wrath = You will be tormented eternally - There is NO REST, no escape, no

This is not a suggestion. This is God's binding declaration.
