PART ONE: THE FOUNDATION
How Scripture Interprets Scripture
The Bible is self-interpreting. When we follow the thread of prophecy across multiple books, the
scattered pieces form a cohesive image. Daniel provides the timeline and kingdoms. Paul (1 & 2
Thessalonians) provides the trigger mechanism. Revelation provides the full picture and outcome.
PART TWO: DANIEL - THE PROPHETIC TIMELINE
Daniel 2: The Four Kingdoms and the Iron-Clay Feet
Daniel 2:37-45 - Nebuchadnezzar's dream interpreted:
- Gold Head = Babylon (606-539 BC) - Silver Chest = Medo-Persia (539-331 BC) - Bronze Belly =
Greece (331-146 BC) - Iron Legs = Rome (146 BC - 476 AD) - Iron & Clay Feet = The final divided
kingdom (from Rome's fall to the end)


---

Key verse: "And whereas thou sawest iron mixed with miry clay, they shall mingle themselves with the
seed of men: but they shall not cleave one to another, even as iron is not mixed with clay." (Daniel
2:43)
Meaning: The final kingdom is DIVIDED, WEAKENED, unable to hold together. This is Papal Rome
and the nations of Europe/the Western world—iron strength mixed with clay weakness, trying to unite
but never fully successful.
Daniel 7: The Four Beasts and the Little Horn
Daniel 7:1-8 - Four beasts paralleling the four kingdoms:
- First Beast = Babylon (like a lion) - Second Beast = Medo-Persia (like a bear) - Third Beast = Greece
(like a leopard) - Fourth Beast = Rome (dreadful, terrible, with iron teeth and ten horns)
The Critical Detail - The Little Horn:
"I considered the horns, and, behold, there came up among them another little horn, before whom there
were three of the first horns plucked up by the roots: and, behold, in this horn were eyes like the eyes of
a man, and a mouth speaking great things." (Daniel 7:8)
Daniel 7:24-25: "And the ten horns out of this kingdom are ten kings that shall arise: and another shall
rise after them; and he shall be diverse from the first, and he shall subdue three kings. And he shall
speak great words against the most High, and shall wear out the saints of the most High, and think to
change times and laws: and they shall be given into his hand until a time and times and the dividing of
time."
Who is the Little Horn? - Rises up among the ten horns (the kingdoms of divided Rome/Europe) -
Speaks great words against the Most High - Wears out the saints - Thinks to change times and
laws (changed Sabbath to Sunday, etc.) - Has dominion for "a time, times, and the dividing of time"
(1,260 years / 42 months)
This is Papal Rome. The system that emerged from the collapse of the Roman Empire in the 5th-6th
century, claiming religious and political authority.
Daniel 8: The Ram, the Goat, and the Little Horn (Revisited)
Daniel 8:9 describes another "little horn" context in the latter days: "And out of one of them came forth
a little horn, which waxed exceeding great, toward the south, and toward the east, and toward the
pleasant land."
This vision also points to a power that magnifies itself even to the Prince of the Host (8:11) and takes
away the daily sacrifice.


---

Daniel 11:36-45: The King of the North in the Latter Days
Daniel 11:36: "And the king shall do according to his will; and he shall exalt himself, and magnify
himself above every god, and shall speak marvellous things against the God of gods, and shall prosper
till the indignation be accomplished: for that that is determined shall be done."
Daniel 11:40: "And at the time of the end shall the king of the south push at him: and the king of the
north shall come against him like a whirlwind..."
The "time of the end" is explicitly mentioned. The prophecies of Daniel are sealed for this specific
time period.
Daniel 12: The Sealing Until the Time of the End
Daniel 12:4: "But thou, O Daniel, shut up the words, and seal the book, even to the time of the end:
many shall run to and fro, and knowledge shall be increased."
Daniel 12:9-10: "And he said, Go thy way, Daniel: for the words are closed up and sealed till the time
of the end. Many shall be purified, and made white, and tried; but the wicked shall do wickedly: and
none of the wicked shall understand; but the wise shall understand."
This is crucial: Daniel's prophecies are sealed UNTIL the time of the end. When we reach the end
times, these prophecies become clear and understandable.
We are in that time now.
PART THREE: 1 THESSALONIANS 5 - THE TRIGGER SIGNAL
1 Thessalonians 5:1-3: The Day of the Lord and Peace and Safety
1 Thessalonians 5:1-2: "But of the times and the seasons, brethren, ye have no need that I write unto
you. For yourselves know perfectly that the day of the Lord so cometh as a thief in the night."
1 Thessalonians 5:3 - THE KEY VERSE: "For when they shall say, Peace and safety; then sudden

The Critical Connection
Notice the "travail upon a woman with child" language. This is a DIRECT REFERENCE to
Revelation 12:2.
This is Scripture interpreting Scripture.


---

Paul is saying: When the world declares "Peace and Safety," that is the signal that sudden destruction
is coming. And he uses the same image as Revelation—the woman in travail/labor pains—to
describe the acceleration of end-time events.
What Is "Peace and Safety"?
In 2026, we see it happening in real time:

This matches perfectly. The declaration of "Peace and Safety" is the warning signal that sudden

PART FOUR: 2 THESSALONIANS - THE MAN OF SIN REVEALED
2 Thessalonians 2:1-12: The Day of Christ and the Man of Sin
2 Thessalonians 2:2-3: "That ye be not soon shaken in mind, or be troubled, neither by spirit, nor by
word, nor by letter as from us, as that the day of Christ is at hand. Let no man deceive you by any
means: for that day shall not come, except there come a falling away first, and that man of sin be
revealed, the son of perdition;"
What must come first: 1. A falling away (apostasy - departure from truth) 2. The man of sin
revealed (the son of perdition)
2 Thessalonians 2:3-4: "Who opposeth and exalteth himself above all that is called God, or that is
worshipped; so that he as God sitteth in the temple of God, shewing himself that he is God."
Who is the Man of Sin?
This describes a system that: - Opposes God's authority - Exalts itself above all that is called God -
Sits as God in the temple of God (claiming God's authority) - Shows himself as God (claiming divine
powers, like forgiving sins)
This is the Papal system.
The Pope claims to: - Forgive sins (only Christ can do this) - Change God's laws (changed the Sabbath
to Sunday) - Speak infallibly for God - Sit in a position of supreme spiritual authority
The Papal system already sits as God in the temple (the Church). This prophecy IS fulfilled.

2 Thessalonians 2:8-12: The Power and the Deception
2 Thessalonians 2:8-9: "And then shall that Wicked be revealed, whom the Lord shall consume with
the spirit of his mouth, and shall destroy with the brightness of his coming: Even him, whose coming is
after the working of Satan with all power and signs and lying wonders,"
2 Thessalonians 2:10-12: "And with all deceivableness of unrighteousness in them that perish; because
they received not the love of the truth, that they might be saved. And for this cause God shall send them
strong delusion, that they should believe a lie: That they all might be damned who believed not the
truth, but had pleasure in unrighteousness."
The Mechanism
- "Working of Satan with all power and signs and lying wonders" - Satanic miracles and deceptions
- "Strong delusion" - God allows people to be deceived if they reject truth - "Believe a lie" - They

governance, backed by religious authority and lies.
PART FIVE: REVELATION - THE FULL PICTURE
Revelation 12: The Woman in Travail
Revelation 12:1-2: "And there appeared a great wonder in heaven; a woman clothed with the sun, and
the moon under her feet, and upon her head a crown of twelve stars: And she being with child cried,
travailing in birth, and pained to be delivered."
This is the labor of the end times. Not a slow, steady process, but labor pains that intensify and
come faster as delivery (Christ's return) approaches.
Paul references this exact image when he says "as travail upon a woman with child"—he's directly
connecting the Peace and Safety declaration to the final labor pains of human history.
Revelation 13: The Two Beasts
Revelation 13:1-7 - The First Beast (Papal Rome):
"And I stood upon the sand of the sea, and saw a beast rise up out of the sea, having seven heads and
ten horns, and upon his horns ten crowns, and upon his heads the name of blasphemy... And the dragon
gave him his power, and his seat, and great authority."


---

Identifying Characteristics: - Has seven heads and ten horns (the kingdoms of Rome and its
divisions) - "Blasphemies" - Claims that belong to God alone - Given the dragon's power and seat -
Satanic authority - "Power was given unto him to continue forty and two months" (1,260 years -
corresponds to Daniel's timeline)
This is Papal Rome - the religious/political system that emerged from the fallen Roman Empire.
Revelation 13:11-15 - The Second Beast (The United States):
"And I beheld another beast coming up out of the earth; and he had two horns like a lamb, and he spake
as a dragon... And he causeth all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark
in their right hand, or in their foreheads..."
Identifying Characteristics: - Comes from "the earth" (the new world) - Looks like a lamb (appears
peaceful/religious) - Speaks as a dragon (its actions are deceptive) - Exercises all the power of the
first beast - It ENFORCES the system of Papal Rome - Makes the world worship the first beast -
Enforces the mark of the beast
This is America - the military/economic power that will enforce the religious system of Rome globally.
Revelation 13:16-18: The Mark of the Beast
Revelation 13:16-17: "And he causeth all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to
receive a mark in their right hand, or in their foreheads: And that no man might buy or sell, save he that
had the mark, or the name of the beast, or the number of his name."
The Mechanism: - Everyone must receive the mark - "No one can buy or sell" without it - This is
absolute economic control
The Board of Peace framework establishes the infrastructure for this. A global governance system,
digitized currency, global commerce controls—all justified as "peace and safety."
Revelation 14: The Three Angels' Messages
Revelation 14:6-7 - First Angel: "And I saw another angel fly in the midst of heaven, having the
everlasting gospel to preach unto them that dwell on the earth, and to every nation, and kindred, and
tongue, and people, Saying with a loud voice, Fear God, and give glory to him; for the hour of his
judgment is come: and worship him that made heaven, and earth, and the sea, and the fountains of
waters."
Revelation 14:8 - Second Angel: "And there followed another angel, saying, Babylon is fallen, is
fallen, that great city, because she made all nations drink of the wine of the wrath of her fornication."
Revelation 14:9-11 - Third Angel (The Warning): "And the third angel followed them, saying with a
loud voice, If any man worship the beast and his image, and receive his mark in his forehead, or in his


---

hand, The same shall drink of the wine of the wrath of God, which is poured out without mixture into
the cup of his indignation; and he shall be tormented with fire and brimstone in the presence of the holy
angels, and in the presence of the Lamb: And the smoke of their torment ascendeth up for ever and
ever: and they have no rest day nor night, who worship the beast and his image, and whosoever
receiveth the mark of his name."
This is God's final warning before the mark is enforced.

Part IV: Prophecy
Chapter 8: The Nine Converging Signs
COMPREHENSIVE END-TIMES STUDY
The Complete Biblical Timeline and Current Convergence
Using Scripture to Interpret Scripture
PART I: FOUNDATIONAL PRINCIPLES
The Methodology: Bible Interprets Bible
This study uses one principle exclusively: Scripture provides its own definitions, time conversions,
theological frameworks, and interpretations. No external scholarly systems are imposed.
Scripture itself contains: - Its own genealogies with specific numbers - Its own time conversion
principles - Its own prophetic patterns - Its own definitions of terms - Its own fulfillment templates
When Scripture repeats something, it is establishing a principle. When Scripture defines a term, we use
that definition. When Scripture provides a calculation, we perform that calculation.
PART II: GOD'S PROPHETIC CALENDAR
The Base Conversion Rate: 1,000 Years = 1 Day
2 Peter 3:8 - "But do not forget this one thing, dear friends: With the Lord a day is like a thousand
years, and a thousand years are like a day."


---

Psalm 90:4 - "For a thousand years in your sight are like a day that has just gone by, or like a watch in
the night."
This is not metaphorical poetry about God's perspective on time. This is the prophetic conversion rate
for God's timeline. Scripture repeats it to establish it as a principle.
The Template: 6 Days Creation + 7th Day Sabbath Rest
Genesis 2:2-3 - "By the seventh day God had finished the work he had been doing; so on the seventh
day he rested from all his work. Then God blessed the seventh day and made it holy, because on it he
rested from all the work of creating that he had done."
The structure God established: - 6 days of work/creation - 7th day of rest/restoration - This becomes the
template for human history
Converting to God's timeline: - 6 days × 1,000 years per day = 6,000 years of human history - 7th day
× 1,000 years per day = 1,000-year Sabbath rest (the Millennium)
God's calendar shows human history as a 6,000-year period culminating in the Millennium (Day 7).
PART III: THE GENEALOGICAL CALCULATION
From Creation to Christ
Genesis 5 and Genesis 11 provide the genealogies with specific ages when fathers begat sons.
When these genealogies are added: - Adam to Noah: ~1,656 years - Noah to Abraham: ~292 years -
Abraham to David: ~1,010 years - David to Christ: ~1,050 years
Total: Approximately 4,000 years from Adam to Jesus
Converting to God's timeline: - 4,000 years ÷ 1,000 years per day = 4 days of human history completed
The Baptism Date: 27 AD (Daniel's Prophecy Fulfilled)
Daniel 9:24-27 - "Seventy sevens are decreed for your people and your holy city to finish
transgression, to put an end to sin, to atone for wickedness, to bring in everlasting righteousness, to seal
up vision and prophecy and to anoint the most holy person. Know and understand this: From the time
the word goes out to restore and rebuild Jerusalem until the Anointed One, the ruler, comes, there will
be seven sevens and sixty-two sevens."
The calculation: - 7 sevens + 62 sevens = 69 sevens - Each "seven" = 7 years (the day-for-year
principle: Numbers 14:34, Ezekiel 4:6) - 69 sevens = 483 years - Commandment to restore Jerusalem


---

issued: ~445 BC - 445 BC + 483 years = 27-28 AD
Luke 3:1-2 - "In the fifteenth year of the reign of Tiberius Caesar... John the Baptist came preaching in
the wilderness of Judea."
Tiberius's reign began AD 14. The fifteenth year = AD 27-28.
Acts 10:37-38 - "You know what has happened throughout the province of Judea, beginning in Galilee
after the baptism that John proclaimed. How God anointed Jesus of Nazareth with the Holy Spirit and
power."
Jesus was anointed (baptized) at the exact moment Daniel prophesied—27 AD. Scripture itself
pinpointed this date 600 years before it occurred.
From Christ to 2027 AD
From Jesus's baptism (27 AD) to 2027 AD = 2,000 years
Converting to God's timeline: - 2,000 years ÷ 1,000 years per day = 2 days
The Complete Timeline
Day 1-4 (4,000 years): Adam to Jesus's baptism (27 AD) Day 5-6 (2,000 years): Jesus's baptism (27
AD) to 2027 AD Total: Day 1-6 = 6,000 years of human history
2027 AD = Threshold of Day 7 (the Millennium)
PART IV: HOSEA 6:2 AND THE RESURRECTION PATTERN
The Scripture
Hosea 6:2 - "After two days he will revive us; on the third day he will restore us, that we may live in
his sight."
Why This Pattern Applies to End Times
Jesus connected this pattern directly to the end times:
Matthew 12:40 - "For as Jonah was three days and three nights in the belly of a huge fish, so the Son of
Man will be three days and three nights in the heart of the earth."


---

Matthew 16:4 - "A wicked and adulterous generation looks for a sign, and none will be given it except
the sign of Jonah."
Luke 11:29-30 - "The crowds increasing, Jesus said, 'This is a wicked generation. It asks for a sign, but
none will be given it except the sign of Jonah. For as Jonah was a sign to the Ninevites, so also will the
Son of Man be to this generation.'"
Scripture shows the three-day resurrection pattern: 1. Occurs literally in Jonah's experience (3 days in
the fish) 2. Fulfilled in Jesus's death and resurrection (3 days in the tomb) 3. Applied prophetically to
the end times (Hosea 6:2 pattern)
Application to Current Timeline
Hosea 6:2 applied prophetically: - Two days = 2,000 years (using 1,000 years = 1 day conversion) -
Third day = 1,000-year Millennium, restoration, Sabbath rest
From Jesus's baptism (27 AD): - 27 AD + 2,000 years = 2027 AD - 2027 AD marks the end of "two
days" and the beginning of the "third day" - The third day = The Millennium, restoration, eternal
Sabbath rest
This is not prediction. This is reading what Scripture already calculated.
PART V: THREE BIBLICAL DEFINITIONS OF "GENERATION"
Scripture uses "generation" three different ways. Each definition appears multiple times and has been
fulfilled or is being fulfilled.
Definition 1: Beginning Generation = 100 Years
Genesis 15:13-16 - "Then the Lord said to him, 'Know for certain that for four hundred years your
descendants will be enslaved and mistreated in a foreign country... In the fourth generation, they will
come back here.'"
The calculation: - 400 years ÷ 4 generations = 100 years per generation - This definition refers to
extended family lineages
Status: FULFILLED - This occurred during Israel's slavery in Egypt (1445-1045 BC, approximately
400 years, spanning 4 generations of family leadership)
Definition 2: Middle Generation = 40 Years
Matthew 24:34 - "Truly I tell you, this generation will certainly not pass away until all these things
have happened."


---

Context: Jesus spoke these words around 27-30 AD, referring to the signs He had just described (wars,
earthquakes, famines, the gospel being preached to all nations, persecution, the love of many growing
cold).
Historical fulfillment: - Jesus spoke: ~27-30 AD - Temple destroyed: 70 AD - Time span:
Approximately 40 years - All the signs Jesus described occurred within that 40-year period
Status: FULFILLED - Jesus's statement was proven exactly true. The generation that heard His words
experienced all those things before the generation passed away (approximately 40 years later).
This definition represents the span of active adult life in a historical moment.
Definition 3: End Generation = 70-80 Years
Psalm 90:10 - "The length of our days is seventy years—or eighty, if we have the strength; yet the best
of them are but trouble and toil, for they quickly pass, and we fly away."
This verse defines the natural human lifespan in a generation.
Application to the end times:
When Scripture says "this generation shall not pass away," it refers to people alive at a specific marker
event.
The marker event: Israel's restoration as a nation
Israel restored as a sovereign nation: 1948
Using the 70-80 year definition: - 1948 + 70 years = 2017 - 1948 + 80 years = 2027 - Current year:
2026 - 1948 to 2026 = 78 years
We are currently within the end generation (70-80 years from 1948).
Status: IN PROGRESS - The generation born in or before 1948 will witness all these things. Many of
that generation are still alive in 2026.
PART VI: THE FIG TREE PARABLE — MATTHEW 24:32-34
Complete Breakdown Letting Scripture Interpret Scripture
Matthew 24:32-34 - "Now learn this lesson from the fig tree: As soon as its twigs get tender and its
leaves come out, you know that summer is near. Even so, when you see all these things, you know that
it is near, right at the door. Truly I tell you, this generation will certainly not pass away until all these
things have happened."


---

Element 1: The Fig Tree = Israel
Scripture defines what the fig tree represents:
Jeremiah 24:1-6 - "After Nebuchadnezzar king of Babylon had carried off Judah into exile, the Lord
showed me two baskets of figs... 'Like these good figs, I regard as good the exiles from Judah, whom I
sent away from this place to the land of the Babylonians. My eyes will watch over them for their good,
and I will bring them back to this land. I will build them up and not tear them down; I will plant them
and not uproot them.'"
Hosea 9:10 - "When I found Israel, it was like finding grapes in the desert; when I saw your ancestors,
it was like seeing the early fruit on the fig tree."
Micah 4:4 - "Everyone will sit under their own vine and under their own fig tree, and no one will make
them afraid."
John 1:47-50 - "When Jesus saw Nathanael approaching, he said of him, 'Here truly is an Israelite in
whom there is no deceit.' 'How do you know me?' Nathanael asked. Jesus answered, 'I saw you while
you were still under the fig tree before Philip called you.' Then Nathanael declared, 'Rabbi, you are the
Son of God; you are the king of Israel.'"
Scripture consistently uses the fig tree as a symbol of Israel's national status and restoration.
Conclusion: The fig tree = The nation of Israel
Element 2: "Branch Is Yet Tender, Putteth Forth Leaves" = National Restoration
Song of Solomon 2:11-13 - "The winter is past, the rain is over and gone. Flowers appear on the earth;
the season of singing has come... The fig tree forms its early fruit; the blossoming vines spread their
fragrance. Arise, my darling, my beautiful one, come with me."
Joel 2:22 - "Do not be afraid, you wild animals, for the pastures in the wilderness are becoming green.
The trees are bearing their fruit; the fig tree and the vine yield their riches."
Scripture describes putting forth leaves as the season of readiness and renewal.
Conclusion: The branch putting forth leaves = Israel being restored as a functioning nation after
dispersal
Element 3: "Summer Is Nigh" = The Millennium
Matthew 24:32 - "When... its leaves come out, you know that summer is nigh."


---

Luke 21:30-31 - "When they are already budding, you can see for yourselves and know that summer is
near. Even so, when you see these things happening, you know that the kingdom of God is near."
Luke connects "summer" directly to "the kingdom of God."
Micah 4:1-4 - "In the last days the mountain of the Lord's house will be established as the highest of
the mountains... 'He will judge between many peoples and will settle disputes for strong nations far and
wide... Then all will sit under their own vine and under their own fig tree, and no one will make them
afraid, for the Lord has spoken.'"
The Millennial Kingdom is described with fig trees and vines—the imagery of harvest season and
peace.
Revelation 20:1-6 - John describes the thousand-year reign (the Millennium, the Sabbath rest of Day
7).
Conclusion: Summer = The Millennial Kingdom, the final harvest, Day 7 eternal Sabbath rest
Element 4: "All These Things" = The Nine Convergent End-Times Prerequisites
Matthew 24:3-31 lists the specific things that must happen:
Matthew 24:4-5 - False Christs and false prophets will come saying "I am the Christ" Matthew 24:6 -

with power and great glory; angels gathering the elect

PART VIII: THE MARK OF THE BEAST AND GOD'S SEAL
God's Seal: The Sabbath
Exodus 31:13-17 - "Say to the Israelites, 'You must observe my Sabbaths. This will be a sign between
me and you for the generations to come, so you may know that I am the Lord, who makes you holy...
The Israelites are to observe the Sabbath, celebrating it for the generations to come as a lasting
covenant. It will be a sign between me and the Israelites forever, for in six days the Lord made the
heavens and the earth, and on the seventh day he abstained from work and rested.'"
Ezekiel 20:12 - "Also I gave them my Sabbaths as a sign between Us, that they might know that I am
the Lord that sanctify them."
Ezekiel 20:20 - "Hallow My Sabbaths; and they will be a sign between Me and you, that you may
know that I am the Lord your God."
God's seal is the Sabbath—the sign throughout all generations that belongs to God's people.
Why the Sabbath: - Genesis 2:2-3: God rested on the seventh day and sanctified it - The Sabbath
represents God's authority and God's rest - It is given to God's people as a sign of covenant relationship
- It is perpetual: "a sign between me and you throughout your generations"
The Sabbath = Day 7 = The Millennium = 1,000-year eternal rest
God's seal points to the eternal future—the day when God's people rest eternally in God's kingdom.

The Beast's Mark: Revelation 13:16-17
Revelation 13:16-17 - "He causes all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and slave, to receive a
mark on their right hand or on their foreheads, and that no one may buy or sell except one who has the
mark, or the name of the beast, or the number of his name."
Key characteristics of the mark: - It is a literal mark on the hand or forehead - It grants access to all
economic systems (buying/selling) - It is enforced—"causes all" to receive it - It is unavoidable—no
one can buy or sell without it - It represents worship/allegiance to the beast
The technology required for this already exists: - China's digital currency (e-CNY): Operational 6

cameras (China alone) - Social credit systems: Regional pilots 17 years operational, fully formalized 12
years - Digital IDs: Being implemented globally - Biometric tracking: Operational in 60+ nations - The
technical capability to implement "no one can buy or sell" without a digital identifier: NOW EXISTS
The Contrast
God's seal (Sabbath): Points to eternal rest, God's authority, God's covenant with His people, freedom,
sanctification
Beast's mark: Points to temporal control, beast's authority, allegiance to the antichrist, enslavement,
damnation
One grants eternal freedom. The other demands temporal allegiance.

PART X: MATTHEW 24:22 — GOD'S INTERVENTION
The Scripture
Matthew 24:22 - "And except those days should be shortened, there should no flesh be saved: but for
the elect's sake those days shall be shortened."
Decoding the Language (Bible Interprets Bible)
"Those days" = The birth pains period with all nine signs converging
Not a abstract future event, but the specific time period when: - Mark accepted - Birth pains
intensifying - Seal judgments opening - Wars escalating - Famines spreading - Pestilences multiplying -
Persecution accelerating - Love growing cold
"Should be shortened" = Cut short, stopped, halted by divine intervention
The Greek word "kolobao" means to cut short, to amputate, to limit, to shorten. God will take active
steps to stop the progression.
"No flesh be saved" = Complete extinction, zero survivors
If the birth pains continued unchecked at their current acceleration rate, there would be total human
annihilation.
Why: AI-enabled biological weapons, nuclear escalation, environmental collapse, and cascading
system failures would compound so rapidly that human extinction would be mathematically certain.
But the Scripture says: God does not allow this. God intervenes.
"For the elect's sake" = Because of those who believe in Jesus Christ
Scripture defines "the elect":
Matthew 22:14 - "Many are called, but few are chosen."
1 Peter 1:1-2 - "Peter, an apostle of Jesus Christ, to the elect according to the foreknowledge of God
the Father, through sanctification of the Spirit, unto obedience and sprinkling of the blood of Jesus
Christ."
Luke 18:7 - "And shall not God avenge his elect which cry to him day and night?"


---

Romans 8:33 - "Who shall lay anything to the charge of God's elect? It is God that justifieth."
Colossians 3:12 - "Put on therefore, as the elect of God, holy and beloved, bowels of mercies,
kindness, humbleness of mind, meekness, longsuffering."
The elect = Those chosen by God, those who have faith in Jesus Christ, those justified by His blood,
those who cry out to Him.
"Those days shall be shortened" = God WILL intervene and cut short the
tribulation
God will not allow the progression to continue to extinction. He will cut it short.
Complete Meaning
If God did not shorten the birth pains, if He did not intervene in the tribulation, if He allowed the
accelerating convergence to continue unchecked, there would be zero human survivors. Complete
extinction.
But God WILL cut short those days BECAUSE of the elect, because of those who believe in Jesus
Christ and cry out to Him.
God's intervention is not uncertain. It is guaranteed by Scripture. "Those days WILL be
shortened."
PART XI: OBJECTIONS ADDRESSED AND RESOLVED
Objection 1: "Genealogy discrepancies between manuscripts"
Resolution: Use Scripture's genealogies as presented in the text. Genesis 5 and 11 provide the
genealogies. Adding the provided numbers = approximately 4,000 years from Adam to Christ.
Scripture does not require reconciliation with external sources; Scripture interprets Scripture.
Objection 2: "Hosea 6:2 refers to Israel's exile, not end times"
Resolution: Scripture demonstrates dual fulfillment. The three-day pattern occurs: 1. Historically
(Israel's exile and restoration) 2. Literally (Jesus's death and resurrection) 3. Prophetically (end-times
timeline in Hosea 6:2)
Jesus Himself connected the Jonah sign (three days) to the end times in Matthew 12:40, Matthew 16:4,
and Luke 11:29-30. The pattern is valid for both historical and eschatological fulfillment.


---

Objection 3: "Day = 1,000 years is metaphorical, not literal"
Resolution: Scripture uses this principle throughout as a prophetic conversion rate: - 2 Peter 3:8: "A
thousand years like a day" - Psalm 90:4: "A thousand years like a day" - Daniel 9:24-27: Day-for-year
principle (490 days = 490 years) - Numbers 14:34: "A day for a year" - Ezekiel 4:6: "A day for each
year"
Scripture repeats this conversion rate to establish it as a principle. It is not metaphorical; it is the
prophetic time conversion key.
Objection 4: "Why 27 AD baptism instead of birth or crucifixion?"
Resolution: Daniel 9:24-27 prophesied Messiah's ANOINTING, not birth or crucifixion.
Luke 3:1-2 dates the baptism to the 15th year of Tiberius = 27 AD. Acts 10:37-38: "God anointed
Jesus... at baptism."
The baptism/anointing in 27 AD is the fulfillment of Daniel's prophecy. Scripture itself pinpointed this
date 600 years before it occurred. This is not assumption; this is scriptural fulfillment.
Objection 5: "Historical precedent: 1666, 1812, 1918, 1948, Y2K all predicted
wrong"
Resolution: 1. Those were PREDICTIONS made by people guessing about the future 2. We are not
predicting; we are READING what Scripture already calculated 3. Matthew 16:2-3: Jesus rebuked
people for not discerning "the signs of the times." The end-generation CAN and SHOULD know the
times and seasons. 4. 1 Thessalonians 5:1-6: Paul told believers they would know the season ("ye are
not in darkness") 5. Daniel 12:4, 9-10: The book was sealed until the time of the end. "The wise shall
understand."
We are not violating Matthew 24:36 ("no one knows the day or hour"). We are fulfilling Matthew
16:2-3 and 1 Thessalonians 5:1-6 by discerning which SEASON we're in.
The difference between prediction and observation: - Prediction: Guessing about unknown future -
Observation: Reading Scripture's own calculations and matching them to current events
Objection 6: "China's system exists but Revelation 13:16-17 requires truly
global implementation"
Resolution: The technology for global implementation exists and is spreading: - China's e-CNY: 261+
million test users, operational 6 years - Global digital currencies: Spreading through 60+ nations,
100+ more in progress - Deepfake laws: Full enforcement August 2, 2026 (8 months away), creating
infrastructure for mandatory digital identity verification - Biometric systems: Operational in 60+
nations - Surveillance infrastructure: 1 billion+ cameras globally - AI integration: Enabling rapid


---

implementation globally
The technology does not need to be "fully global" on a single day. Revelation describes the system
spreading and becoming normative. This is happening now.
Objection 7: "Futurist interpretation of Daniel's 70 weeks"
Resolution: The 70th week is not future; it is historical: - Daniel 9:24-27 describes Messiah's anointing
and the Temple's destruction - Fulfilled in 27 AD (baptism/anointing) and 70 AD (Temple
destruction) - This is not a prophecy waiting in the future; it already occurred
The birth pains are not a predetermined 7-year event. They are the actual unfolding of real-time
judgment as the mark systems are implemented NOW.

REVELATION UNVEILED
A Complete Biblical Commentary

February 2026
INTRODUCTION: The Book That Unlocks the End
We are living in the generation that will see the fulfillment of Revelation's final prophecies. The fig tree
has put forth its leaves (Israel reborn in 1948). We are now 78 years into the final generation of 70-80
years (Psalm 90:10). The countdown has begun.
This document exists to provide a complete, systematic understanding of Revelation - not through
human speculation, but by allowing the Bible to interpret itself. Every symbol, every timeline, every
prophecy will be defined by Scripture and verified by history and current events.
The Foundation Principle
2 Peter 1:20-21: "Knowing this first, that no prophecy of the scripture is of any private interpretation.
For the prophecy came not in old time by the will of man: but holy men of God spake as they were
moved by the Holy Ghost."


---

We will not guess. We will not speculate. We will search Scripture for God's own definitions, and then
watch as history confirms what was written.
The Promise of Revelation
Revelation 1:1: "The Revelation of Jesus Christ, which God gave unto him, to shew unto his servants

This book is called "Revelation" - not "Mystery." It is meant to REVEAL, not conceal. God wants His
people to understand.

How This Study Works

PART ONE: THE FOUNDATION
Understanding the Symbols and Timeline
Chapter 1: Biblical Definitions of Prophetic Symbols
Before we begin Revelation, we must establish how the Bible defines its own symbols. These
definitions come directly from Scripture - not human interpretation.
BEASTS = Kingdoms/Nations/Political Powers
Daniel 7:17, 23: "These great beasts, which are four, are four kings, which shall arise out of the
earth... The fourth beast shall be the fourth kingdom upon earth."


---

The Bible clearly states: beasts represent kingdoms or political powers.
WATERS/SEA = Peoples, Multitudes, Nations
Revelation 17:15: "The waters which thou sawest, where the whore sitteth, are peoples, and
multitudes, and nations, and tongues."
God defines this for us directly in Revelation itself. Waters represent dense populations.
EARTH = Sparsely Populated Areas
If "waters" represent dense populations, then "earth" (when contrasted with waters) represents areas
with fewer people - newly settled territories.
WOMAN (PURE) = True Church
2 Corinthians 11:2: "I have espoused you to one husband, that I may present you as a chaste virgin to
Christ."
Ephesians 5:25-27: The church is called Christ's bride.
A pure woman represents God's faithful church.
WOMAN (CORRUPT/HARLOT) = Apostate Church
Ezekiel 16:15-17: God uses an unfaithful woman to represent Israel's apostasy.
Hosea 1-3: The entire book uses Hosea's unfaithful wife to represent Israel's spiritual adultery.
A harlot represents a church that has corrupted herself with false doctrines and alliances with worldly
powers.
HORNS = Kings or Kingdoms
Daniel 7:24: "And the ten horns out of this kingdom are ten kings that shall arise."
Revelation 17:12: "And the ten horns which thou sawest are ten kings."
Horns represent power - specifically, kings or kingdoms.
HEADS = Mountains or Governments


---

Revelation 17:9: "The seven heads are seven mountains, on which the woman sitteth."
Mountains can also represent kingdoms (Jeremiah 51:25, Daniel 2:35, 44-45).
DRAGON = Satan
Revelation 12:9: "And the great dragon was cast out, that old serpent, called the Devil, and Satan,
which deceiveth the whole world."
The Bible explicitly identifies the dragon as Satan.
BABYLON = The False Religious System
The name "Babylon" traces back to Genesis 10-11 and the Tower of Babel - the first organized
rebellion against God. Throughout Scripture, Babylon represents: - Rebellion against God's authority -
False worship systems - Counterfeit religion - Man attempting to reach heaven through his own works
PROPHETIC TIME = Day-for-a-Year Principle
Numbers 14:34: "After the number of the days in which ye searched the land, even forty days, each day
for a year, shall ye bear your iniquities, even forty years."
Ezekiel 4:6: "I have appointed thee each day for a year."
In prophetic/symbolic contexts: - 1 day = 1 year - 42 months = 1,260 days = 1,260 years - Time, times,
and half a time = 3.5 years = 1,260 years
Chapter 2: Where We Are in Prophetic History
Before diving into Revelation verse by verse, we must understand WHERE we are in the timeline.
The Fig Tree Generation
Matthew 24:32-34: "Now learn a parable of the fig tree; When his branch is yet tender, and putteth
forth leaves, ye know that summer is nigh: So likewise ye, when ye shall see all these things, know that
it is near, even at the doors. Verily I say unto you, This generation shall not pass, till all these things be
fulfilled."
The fig tree represents Israel (Jeremiah 24, Hosea 9:10, Joel 1:7).
May 14, 1948: Israel reborn as a nation after 2,000 years - the fig tree "put forth leaves."


---

Psalm 90:10: "The days of our years are threescore years and ten; and if by reason of strength they be
fourscore years."
A biblical generation = 70-80 years.
THE TIMELINE: - 1948 + 70 years = 2017 (generation window opens) - 1948 + 80 years = 2027
(maximum generation boundary) - 2026 = We are currently 78 years into the final generation
Matthew 24:22: "And except those days should be shortened, there should no flesh be saved: but for
the elect's sake those days shall be shortened."
The days SHALL be shortened - we may not reach the full 80 years.
The Deadly Wound Healed
Revelation 13:3: "And I saw one of his heads as it were wounded to death; and his deadly wound was
healed: and all the world wondered after the beast."
- 1798: Pope taken captive by Napoleon - deadly wound inflicted - 1929: Lateran Treaty signed -
Vatican becomes independent state - wound begins healing - 2026: 97 years since the treaty; 100 years
from the beginning of negotiations (1926) - 2029: 100 years from the treaty signing
The wound is healed. The world IS wondering after the beast. Popes now meet with world leaders,
address the UN, and command global influence.
Pope Leo XIV - The Lion Speaks
In 2025, during this exact prophetic window, a new Pope took the name Leo XIV.
"Leo" = Lion (Latin)
Revelation 13:2: "And the beast which I saw was like unto a leopard, and his feet were as the feet of a
bear, and his mouth as the mouth of a lion."
The beast has the mouth of a lion. The mouth speaks. The mouth issues decrees. And now - in the final
generation window - there is literally a LION at the head of the Papacy.
Daniel 7:4: The first beast (Babylon) was represented as a lion. Babylon was the HEAD of gold - the
origin of the mystery religion. Now, as we approach the end, Mystery Babylon (the Papacy) has a
LION at its head once again.
Technology: The Image Can Speak
Revelation 13:15: "And he had power to give life unto the image of the beast, that the image of the
beast should both speak, and cause that as many as would not worship the image of the beast should be


---

killed."
The image is given "life" (Greek: pneuma - breath/spirit) and can SPEAK.
Genesis 2:7: "And the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils
the breath of life; and man became a living soul."
When God breathed into man, man could SPEAK.
2026 REALITY: Artificial Intelligence has been created. AI can: - Speak and communicate - Make
decisions - Control financial systems - Identify individuals through facial recognition - Execute
economic sanctions
The technology to give the image "breath" and the ability to "speak" and enforce economic sanctions
EXISTS RIGHT NOW.
PART TWO: REVELATION 1-3
The Vision of Christ and the Seven Churches
Chapter 3: Revelation 1 - The Vision of Christ
Verse 1:1 - The Purpose
"The Revelation of Jesus Christ, which God gave unto him, to shew unto his servants things
which must shortly come to pass; and he sent and signified it by his angel unto his servant John:"
This is not "John's Revelation" - it is the Revelation of JESUS CHRIST. God the Father gave it to
Jesus, who sent it through an angel to John.
"Signified" - from Greek semaino - meaning "to give a sign" or "to signify by symbols." This tells us
the book uses SYMBOLS that must be interpreted.
"Shortly come to pass" - From God's eternal perspective, 2,000 years is short. But also - once the final
events BEGIN, they will happen rapidly.
APPLICATION TO 2026: The events are beginning NOW. We are in the generation that will see "all
these things" fulfilled (Matthew 24:34).
Verses 1:3 - The Blessing


---

"Blessed is he that readeth, and they that hear the words of this prophecy, and keep those things
which are written therein: for the time is at hand."
Three actions bring blessing: 1. Reading it 2. Hearing it (understanding it) 3. Keeping (obeying) what
it says
"The time is at hand" - When John wrote this in ~95 AD, it was future. Now, 2,000 years later, we ARE
at that time. The clock has started.
Verses 1:4-8 - Grace, Glory, and the Second Coming
Verse 7: "Behold, he cometh with clouds; and every eye shall see him, and they also which pierced
him: and all kindreds of the earth shall wail because of him. Even so, Amen."
This is Jesus' Second Coming - referenced immediately in chapter 1. The entire book builds toward this
event.
APPLICATION: The Second Coming is the culmination of all prophecy. Everything in Revelation
moves toward this moment.
Verses 1:9-11 - John's Vision Begins
"I John, who also am your brother, and companion in tribulation, and in the kingdom and
patience of Jesus Christ, was in the isle that is called Patmos, for the word of God, and for the
testimony of Jesus Christ."
John was exiled to Patmos (a Roman prison island) for preaching God's Word. Even in exile, God gave
him the greatest prophetic vision in Scripture.
"I was in the Spirit on the Lord's day" - John was in prophetic vision on the Sabbath (the Lord's day
- see Isaiah 58:13, Mark 2:28).
Verses 1:12-20 - The Vision of Christ
John sees seven golden candlesticks (lampstands) and Christ in the midst of them.
Verse 20: "The mystery of the seven stars which thou sawest in my right hand, and the seven golden
candlesticks. The seven stars are the angels of the seven churches: and the seven candlesticks which
thou sawest are the seven churches."
God interprets His own symbols: - 7 stars = angels (messengers/leaders) of the seven churches - 7
candlesticks = the seven churches
The churches are LAMPSTANDS - called to bear light (God's truth) to the world.


---

Chapter 4: Revelation 2-3 - The Seven Churches (Prophetic Church History)
The seven churches in Revelation 2-3 are: 1. Real, literal churches that existed in John's day 2.
Messages applicable to Christians in all ages 3. Prophetic outline of church history from the
apostolic age to the end
The Seven Churches as Prophetic Timeline
Church | Meaning | Time Period | Characteristics | Status in 2026
Ephesus | "Desirable" | 31-100 AD | Apostolic church, lost first love | FULFILLED Smyrna | "Myrrh"
(persecution) | 100-313 AD | Persecuted under Rome | FULFILLED Pergamos | "Elevation" | 313-538
AD | Church elevated to power (Constantine) | FULFILLED Thyatira | "Continual sacrifice" |
538-1517 AD | Papal supremacy, Dark Ages | FULFILLED Sardis | "Remnant" | 1517-1798 AD |
Reformation, but incomplete | FULFILLED Philadelphia | "Brotherly love" | 1798-1844 AD | Great
missionary movement | FULFILLED Laodicea | "Judgment of the people" | 1844-Second Coming |
Lukewarm, last church | CURRENT
Why This Matters for 2026
We are living in the Laodicean age - the final church period before Christ returns. Let's examine this
church closely.
LAODICEA - The Church of 2026
Revelation 3:14-22 - The Message to Laodicea
Verse 3:14
"And unto the angel of the church of the Laodiceans write; These things saith the Amen, the
faithful and true witness, the beginning of the creation of God;"
"Laodicea" means "judgment of the people" or "the people judging." This church period coincides
with: - The investigative judgment in heaven (Daniel 7:9-10, Revelation 14:7) - The time when people
judge FOR THEMSELVES what is truth (dangerous - see Proverbs 14:12)
Verses 3:15-16 - The Lukewarm Condition
"I know thy works, that thou art neither cold nor hot: I would thou wert cold or hot. So then
because thou art lukewarm, and neither cold nor hot, I will spue thee out of my mouth."
LUKEWARM - Not on fire for God, but not openly hostile either. Comfortable. Complacent. Going
through the motions.


---

APPLICATION TO 2026: - Church attendance declining in Western nations - Doctrinal compromise
to avoid offending - "Seeker-friendly" churches that avoid hard truths - Entertainment-based worship
rather than reverence - Social gospel replacing the everlasting gospel - Churches accepting practices the
Bible condemns
The church in 2026 is EXACTLY as Jesus described: lukewarm.
Verse 3:17 - The Deception
"Because thou sayest, I am rich, and increased with goods, and have need of nothing; and
knowest not that thou art wretched, and miserable, and poor, and blind, and naked:"
SELF-DECEPTION: Laodicea thinks it's doing great. "We have large buildings, big budgets, full
programs - we're blessed!"
GOD'S VERDICT: Wretched, miserable, poor, blind, naked.
APPLICATION TO 2026: - Megachurches with massive budgets but little spiritual power - Prosperity
gospel: "God wants you rich!" - Entertainment-driven services that lack the Holy Spirit - Biblical
illiteracy even among regular church attenders - Moral compromise to "stay relevant"
The church is spiritually BANKRUPT while thinking it's wealthy.
Verses 3:18 - The Remedy
"I counsel thee to buy of me gold tried in the fire, that thou mayest be rich; and white raiment,
that thou mayest be clothed, and that the shame of thy nakedness do not appear; and anoint thine
eyes with eyesalve, that thou mayest see."
Jesus offers three things:
1. Gold tried in the fire = Faith and love (1 Peter 1:7, 1 Corinthians 13) 2. White raiment = Christ's
righteousness (Revelation 19:8) 3. Eyesalve = Spiritual discernment through the Holy Spirit
APPLICATION: What the church needs in 2026 is not better programs or bigger buildings - it needs
genuine faith, Christ's righteousness, and spiritual discernment to see the times.
Verse 3:20 - Jesus Outside His Own Church
"Behold, I stand at the door, and knock: if any man hear my voice, and open the door, I will come
in to him, and will sup with him, and he with me."
The most tragic verse in Revelation: Jesus is standing OUTSIDE His own church, knocking, trying to
get in.


---

In every other church, Jesus is inside. Only in Laodicea is He locked out.
APPLICATION TO 2026: Jesus is not welcome in many churches today: - His hard sayings are
avoided - His commandments are taught as "legalism" - His call to holiness is replaced with
"acceptance" - His warnings of judgment are considered "negative"
But He's still knocking. Individual response is what matters - "if ANY MAN hear my voice."
The Overcomers' Promise (Verse 3:21)
"To him that overcometh will I grant to sit with me in my throne, even as I also overcame, and
am set down with my Father in his throne."
Those who overcome in this lukewarm age will receive the greatest reward: sharing Christ's throne.
Why? Because overcoming in Laodicea is HARD. When everyone around you is lukewarm, staying on
fire for God requires tremendous faith.
PART THREE: REVELATION 4-5
The Throne Room of Heaven
Chapter 5: Revelation 4 - The Throne and the 24 Elders
Verse 4:1 - A Door Opened in Heaven
"After this I looked, and, behold, a door was opened in heaven: and the first voice which I heard
was as it were of a trumpet talking with me; which said, Come up hither, and I will shew thee
things which must be hereafter."
The scene shifts from earth (the seven churches) to heaven. John is shown what is happening in the
throne room of God.
"Things which must be hereafter" - Future events from John's perspective (still future for us in some
cases).
Verses 4:2-3 - The Throne
"And immediately I was in the spirit: and, behold, a throne was set in heaven, and one sat on the
throne. And he that sat was to look upon like a jasper and a sardine stone: and there was a


---

rainbow round about the throne, in sight like unto an emerald."
God is on the throne. The rainbow speaks of His covenant promises (Genesis 9:13-16).
CRITICAL POINT: No matter what chaos unfolds on earth, GOD IS STILL ON THE THRONE. He
is in control.
Verses 4:4 - The 24 Elders
"And round about the throne were four and twenty seats: and upon the seats I saw four and
twenty elders sitting, clothed in white raiment; and they had on their heads crowns of gold."
Who are the 24 elders? Scripture gives us clues:
1. They are sitting (position of rest/completion) 2. They wear white raiment (righteousness/victory) 3.
They have crowns (Greek: stephanos - victor's crown) 4. They are redeemed (Revelation 5:9-10)
These represent the redeemed from both Old Testament and New Testament - 12 tribes + 12 apostles =
24.
Matthew 27:52-53: "And the graves were opened; and many bodies of the saints which slept arose,
And came out of the graves after his resurrection, and went into the holy city, and appeared unto
many."
When Christ rose, He took captivity captive (Ephesians 4:8) - these are likely those resurrected saints
who ascended with Him.
Verses 4:6-8 - The Four Living Creatures
The four living creatures have: - Face of a lion (king of wild beasts - majesty) - Face of a calf/ox
(servant - strength) - Face of a man (intelligence - humanity) - Face of an eagle (divinity - soaring
above)
These represent the four aspects of Christ's ministry in the Gospels: - Matthew: Lion - Christ as King -
Mark: Ox - Christ as Servant - Luke: Man - Christ as perfect human - John: Eagle - Christ as divine
Son of God
The Continuous Worship (Verse 4:8)
"And they rest not day and night, saying, Holy, holy, holy, LORD God Almighty, which was, and
is, and is to come."
The throne room of heaven is filled with continuous worship. While earth rebels, heaven worships.


---

Chapter 6: Revelation 5 - The Lamb and the Sealed Book
Verses 5:1-4 - The Sealed Book
"And I saw in the right hand of him that sat on the throne a book written within and on the
backside, sealed with seven seals... And I wept much, because no man was found worthy to open
and to read the book, neither to look thereon."
A book (scroll) sealed with seven seals appears. No one in heaven or earth is worthy to open it. John
weeps because this book contains the future of earth - and no one can reveal it.
Verses 5:5-6 - The Lion Who Is a Lamb
"Weep not: behold, the Lion of the tribe of Juda, the Root of David, hath prevailed to open the
book... And I beheld, and, lo, in the midst of the throne... stood a Lamb as it had been slain."
Jesus is called BOTH: - The Lion (power, majesty, kingship) - The Lamb (sacrifice, meekness,
redemption)
He conquered as a Lion BY BEING a Lamb - through sacrifice, not force.
Note: In 2025, Pope Leo XIV takes the name "Lion" - but he has the WRONG kind of power. He
claims authority like a lion, but WITHOUT the sacrifice of the Lamb. This is the counterfeit.
Verses 5:9-10 - The Song of the Redeemed
"Thou art worthy to take the book, and to open the seals thereof: for thou wast slain, and hast
redeemed us to God by thy blood out of every kindred, and tongue, and people, and nation; And
hast made us unto our God kings and priests: and we shall reign on the earth."
The 24 elders sing "thou hast redeemed US" - proving they are redeemed humans, not angels.
PART FOUR: REVELATION 6-8
The Seven Seals - Church History Revealed
Chapter 7: Understanding the Seven Seals
The seven seals represent the same time period as the seven churches - FROM the apostolic age TO the
Second Coming - but from a DIFFERENT perspective. The churches show the INTERNAL spiritual
condition; the seals show the EXTERNAL persecution and trials.


---

THE SEVEN SEALS
FIRST SEAL - White Horse (Revelation 6:1-2)
"And I saw, and behold a white horse: and he that sat on him had a bow; and a crown was given
unto him: and he went forth conquering, and to conquer."
TIME PERIOD: 31-100 AD (Apostolic church) PARALLEL CHURCH: Ephesus
SYMBOLISM: - White = Purity, victory - Horse = Warfare/conquest (in prophecy - Jeremiah 8:6,
Zechariah 10:3) - Bow = Weapon of warfare - Crown = Victory
FULFILLMENT: The apostolic church went forth conquering through the gospel. They conquered
hearts, not nations. The gospel spread rapidly throughout the Roman Empire despite persecution.
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED
SECOND SEAL - Red Horse (Revelation 6:3-4)
"And there went out another horse that was red: and power was given to him that sat thereon to
take peace from the earth, and that they should kill one another: and there was given unto him a
great sword."
TIME PERIOD: 100-313 AD (Persecution under pagan Rome) PARALLEL CHURCH: Smyrna
("myrrh" - crushed/persecuted)
SYMBOLISM: - Red = Blood, martyrdom - Take peace from earth = Persecution - Great sword =
Execution, violence
FULFILLMENT: The age of martyrs. Ten major persecutions under Roman emperors (Nero,
Domitian, Trajan, Marcus Aurelius, Septimius Severus, Maximinus, Decius, Valerian, Aurelian,
Diocletian). Christians were fed to lions, burned alive, crucified. Blood stained the Roman Empire red.
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED
THIRD SEAL - Black Horse (Revelation 6:5-6)
"And I beheld, and lo a black horse; and he that sat on him had a pair of balances in his hand.
And I heard a voice in the midst of the four beasts say, A measure of wheat for a penny, and three
measures of barley for a penny; and see thou hurt not the oil and the wine."
TIME PERIOD: 313-538 AD (Church elevated to power) PARALLEL CHURCH: Pergamos
("elevation")


---

SYMBOLISM: - Black = Darkness, famine (spiritual famine of truth) - Balances = Commercialism,
weighing/measuring - Wheat/barley = Food (spiritual food - God's Word) - Penny = Day's wages
(costly) - Oil and wine = Holy Spirit and truth (preserved in remnant)
FULFILLMENT: When Constantine "converted" to Christianity (313 AD), he elevated the church to
power and wealth. BUT this was spiritual darkness: - Pagan practices entered the church - Truth
became "expensive" - restricted to clergy - Doctrines were weighed and measured by church councils,
not Scripture - The pure oil (Spirit) and wine (truth) were preserved only in faithful remnants
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED
FOURTH SEAL - Pale Horse (Revelation 6:7-8)
"And I looked, and behold a pale horse: and his name that sat on him was Death, and Hell
followed with him. And power was given unto them over the fourth part of the earth, to kill with
sword, and with hunger, and with death, and with the beasts of the earth."
TIME PERIOD: 538-1517 AD (Dark Ages of papal supremacy) PARALLEL CHURCH: Thyatira
("continual sacrifice")
SYMBOLISM: - Pale (Greek: chloros - pale green, sickly) - Death and Hell = Spiritual and physical
death - Fourth part of earth = Western Europe under papal control - Sword, hunger, death, beasts =
Methods of persecution
FULFILLMENT: The Dark Ages. The Papacy ruled with absolute power for 1,260 years (538-1798
AD). Millions died: - The Inquisition tortured and burned "heretics" - The Crusades killed in the name
of Christ - Waldenses, Albigenses, Huguenots massacred - Anyone with a Bible in their own language
was executed - Conservative estimates: 50-150 million martyrs
This was the deadliest period in church history.
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED
FIFTH SEAL - Souls Under the Altar (Revelation 6:9-11)
"And when he had opened the fifth seal, I saw under the altar the souls of them that were slain
for the word of God, and for the testimony which they held: And they cried with a loud voice,
saying, How long, O Lord, holy and true, dost thou not judge and avenge our blood on them that
dwell on the earth?"
TIME PERIOD: 1517-1755 (Reformation era) PARALLEL CHURCH: Sardis ("remnant")
SYMBOLISM: - Souls under altar = Martyrs crying out for justice - How long? = Patience of the
martyrs waiting for judgment - White robes given = Vindication promised


---

FULFILLMENT: The Reformation began (1517 - Martin Luther). Truth was being restored, but
persecution continued. Millions MORE were martyred by the Papacy during this period. The martyrs
cry out, "How long before You judge our persecutors?"
Answer: "Rest yet for a little season" - judgment is coming, but not yet.
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED
SIXTH SEAL - Great Earthquake and Signs (Revelation 6:12-17)
"And I beheld when he had opened the sixth seal, and, lo, there was a great earthquake; and the
sun became black as sackcloth of hair, and the moon became as blood; And the stars of heaven
fell unto the earth... And the heaven departed as a scroll when it is rolled together."
TIME PERIOD: 1755-Second Coming (Signs in nature pointing to the end) PARALLEL CHURCH:
Philadelphia and Laodicea
SIGNS LISTED: 1. Great earthquake 2. Sun darkened 3. Moon as blood 4. Stars fall 5. Heaven
departs as scroll 6. Mountains and islands moved
HISTORICAL FULFILLMENT (verses 12-13):
1. GREAT EARTHQUAKE (verse 12a) November 1, 1755 - Lisbon Earthquake - Magnitude 9.0 -
Destroyed Lisbon, Portugal - Killed 60,000+ people - Felt across Europe and North Africa - Called "the
earthquake that shook the Enlightenment" - Exactly as prophesied - first sign of the sixth seal
2. SUN DARKENED (verse 12b) May 19, 1780 - The Dark Day - Occurred in New England - Sun
disappeared at midday - Complete darkness covered the land - No scientific explanation (not an eclipse)
- Historical records confirm this event - Candles needed at noon - Exactly as prophesied
3. MOON AS BLOOD (verse 12c) Same night - May 19-20, 1780 - When moon finally appeared that
night, it was blood red - Multiple eyewitness accounts - Exactly as prophesied
4. STARS FALL (verse 13) November 13, 1833 - The Leonid Meteor Shower - Largest meteor
shower in recorded history - Estimated 100,000+ meteors per hour - Visible across North America -
Lasted for hours - Newspapers called it "the night the stars fell" - People thought the world was ending
- Exactly as prophesied - stars fell "as a fig tree casteth her untimely figs"
FUTURE FULFILLMENT (verses 14-17):
5-6. HEAVEN DEPARTS, MOUNTAINS MOVED - This is still FUTURE. These are the cosmic
signs that accompany Christ's Second Coming.
CRITICAL POINT FOR 2026:


---

We are living DURING the sixth seal. Four of the six signs have been FULFILLED (earthquake, dark
sun, blood moon, falling stars). The final two signs (heaven departing, mountains moved) happen AT
Christ's return.
The sixth seal SPANS from 1755 to the Second Coming. We are in this period RIGHT NOW.
SEVENTH SEAL - Silence in Heaven (Revelation 8:1)
"And when he had opened the seventh seal, there was silence in heaven about the space of half an
hour."
TIME: At the Second Coming
SYMBOLISM: - Silence = All of heaven comes to earth with Jesus - Half an hour = In prophetic time
(day = year), half an hour would be about 7 literal days
FULFILLMENT: This seal opens at Christ's return. Every angel leaves heaven to accompany Jesus to
earth (Matthew 25:31). Heaven is SILENT because everyone has come to earth.
STATUS IN 2026: FUTURE - but signs indicate we are very close
Chapter 8: Revelation 7 - The Sealing of the 144,000
Between the sixth and seventh seals, John sees an interlude (Revelation 7).
Verses 7:1-3 - Four Angels Holding Four Winds
"And after these things I saw four angels standing on the four corners of the earth, holding the
four winds of the earth, that the wind should not blow on the earth, nor on the sea, nor on any
tree. And I saw another angel ascending from the east, having the seal of the living God: and he
cried with a loud voice to the four angels, to whom it was given to hurt the earth and the sea,
Saying, Hurt not the earth, neither the sea, nor the trees, till we have sealed the servants of our
God in their foreheads."
BIBLICAL DEFINITION OF "WINDS":
Jeremiah 25:31-33: Winds represent strife, war, judgment
Daniel 7:2: Four winds striving on the sea represent political turmoil
INTERPRETATION:
Four angels are HOLDING BACK the final crisis - preventing global destruction - until God's people
are SEALED.


---

The angel from the east (where the sun rises - Jesus is called the Sun of Righteousness in Malachi 4:2)
commands: "Don't let destruction come until we seal God's servants!"
APPLICATION TO 2026:
This is happening RIGHT NOW. The world is on the brink of: - Nuclear war - Economic collapse -
Pandemic diseases - Civil unrest - Natural disasters
But angels are RESTRAINING these forces until the sealing is complete. That's why the world hasn't
already collapsed - God is giving time for people to make their final decision.
The Seal of God
Verse 3: "till we have sealed the servants of our God in their foreheads"
The seal is in the forehead - representing the MIND, BELIEF, DECISION.
What is God's seal?
Ezekiel 20:12, 20: "Moreover also I gave them my sabbaths, to be a sign between me and them, that
they might know that I am the LORD that sanctify them... And hallow my sabbaths; and they shall be a
sign between me and you, that ye may know that I am the LORD your God."
Exodus 31:16-17: "Wherefore the children of Israel shall keep the sabbath, to observe the sabbath
throughout their generations, for a perpetual covenant. It is a sign between me and the children of
Israel for ever: for in six days the LORD made heaven and earth, and on the seventh day he rested, and
was refreshed."
The Sabbath is God's SIGN (seal) that: - He is the Creator - He has authority to command worship - He
sanctifies His people
The seal contains: 1. Name: The LORD (YHWH) 2. Title: Creator ("made heaven and earth") 3.
Territory: Heaven and earth
This matches the requirements of any official seal - name, title, territory of jurisdiction.
Verses 7:4-8 - The 144,000
"And I heard the number of them which were sealed: and there were sealed an hundred and
forty and four thousand of all the tribes of the children of Israel."
The 144,000 represent: - 12 tribes × 12,000 each = 144,000 - 12 = God's organizational number (12
tribes, 12 apostles, 12 gates) - 1,000 = Completeness, multitude - 144,000 = Complete number of God's
faithful people in the last days


---

These are described in Revelation 14:1-5: - They have Father's name in foreheads (sealed) - They
follow the Lamb wherever He goes - They keep the commandments of God - They have the faith of
Jesus - They are without guile (deception) - They are the firstfruits (first to be fully sealed)
Note: This is likely symbolic of a complete, perfect number - not necessarily a literal count. Just as
"Israel" now includes all who believe in Jesus (Romans 2:28-29, Galatians 3:29), the 144,000 represent
the complete body of end-time believers who are sealed.
Verses 7:9-17 - The Great Multitude
"After this I beheld, and, lo, a great multitude, which no man could number, of all nations, and
kindreds, and people, and tongues, stood before the throne, and before the Lamb, clothed with
white robes, and palms in their hands."
After the numbered 144,000, John sees an INNUMERABLE multitude. These are the redeemed from
all ages.
Verse 14: "These are they which came out of great tribulation, and have washed their robes, and made
them white in the blood of the Lamb."
All the saved - from every age - have come through "great tribulation." They are saved by grace
through faith in Jesus' blood, not by their own works.
PART FIVE: REVELATION 12-13
The Great Controversy - The Woman, the Dragon, and the Beasts
This is the HEART of Revelation. Here we see the complete picture of the war between Christ and
Satan, played out through history and climaxing in our day.
Chapter 9: Revelation 12 - The Woman and the Dragon
Revelation 12 is the KEY to understanding the entire book. It traces the great controversy from its
beginning in heaven to its climax on earth.
Verses 12:1-2 - The Pure Woman (God's Church)
"And there appeared a great wonder in heaven; a woman clothed with the sun, and the moon
under her feet, and upon her head a crown of twelve stars: And she being with child cried,
travailing in birth, and pained to be delivered."


---

BIBLICAL DEFINITION: Woman = Church (2 Corinthians 11:2, Ephesians 5:25-27)
SYMBOLISM: - Clothed with the sun = Clothed with Christ's righteousness (Malachi 4:2 - "Sun of
righteousness") - Moon under feet = Standing on the foundation of the Old Testament (moon reflects
sun's light; OT reflects Christ) - Crown of 12 stars = 12 tribes/12 apostles - complete church - With
child = About to bring forth the Messiah
This is God's faithful church through the ages, about to bring forth Christ.
Verses 12:3-4 - The Red Dragon (Satan)
"And there appeared another wonder in heaven; and behold a great red dragon, having seven
heads and ten horns, and seven crowns upon his heads. And his tail drew the third part of the
stars of heaven, and did cast them to the earth: and the dragon stood before the woman which
was ready to be delivered, for to devour her child as soon as it was born."
BIBLICAL DEFINITION: Verse 9 identifies him: "And the great dragon was cast out, that old
serpent, called the Devil, and Satan, which deceiveth the whole world."
SYMBOLISM: - Red = Blood, murder (John 8:44 - "murderer from the beginning") - Seven heads =
Seven kingdoms Satan has used (Egypt, Assyria, Babylon, Medo-Persia, Greece, Rome, Papal Rome) -
Ten horns = Ten divisions of Rome - Third part of stars = One-third of angels fell with Lucifer
(Isaiah 14:12-15, Ezekiel 28:12-17) - Devour child = Satan working through King Herod to kill baby
Jesus (Matthew 2:16)
Verse 12:5 - The Man Child (Jesus Christ)
"And she brought forth a man child, who was to rule all nations with a rod of iron: and her child
was caught up unto God, and to his throne."
The child is Jesus Christ: - Rules nations with rod of iron (Psalm 2:9, Revelation 19:15) - Caught up to
God's throne (Ascension - Acts 1:9-11)
Verse 12:6 - The 1,260 Years
"And the woman fled into the wilderness, where she hath a place prepared of God, that they
should feed her there a thousand two hundred and threescore days."
1,260 DAYS (using the day-year principle in prophetic context) = 1,260 YEARS
This is the SAME period as: - Daniel 7:25 - "time, times, and half a time" = 1,260 years - Revelation
13:5 - "42 months" = 1,260 years - Revelation 12:14 - "time, times, and half a time" = 1,260 years
HISTORICAL FULFILLMENT: 538 AD - 1798 AD


---

The true church fled into the "wilderness" (sparsely populated areas - mountains of Europe, remote
regions) to escape papal persecution during the Dark Ages.
Groups that preserved truth in the wilderness: - Waldenses (Alps mountains) - Albigenses
(Southern France) - Huguenots (France) - Lollards (England) - Hussites (Bohemia) - Other faithful
groups
Verses 12:7-9 - War in Heaven
"And there was war in heaven: Michael and his angels fought against the dragon; and the dragon
fought and his angels, And prevailed not; neither was their place found any more in heaven. And
the great dragon was cast out, that old serpent, called the Devil, and Satan, which deceiveth the
whole world: he was cast out into the earth, and his angels were cast out with him."
WHO IS MICHAEL?
The name "Michael" means "Who is like God?"
Daniel 12:1: "And at that time shall Michael stand up, the great prince which standeth for thy people"
Jude 1:9: "Yet Michael the archangel, when contending with the devil he disputed about the body of
Moses"
1 Thessalonians 4:16: "For the Lord himself shall descend from heaven with a shout, with the voice of
the archangel, and with the trump of God"
Michael is Jesus Christ - the Archangel, the Commander of heaven's armies.
This war happened BEFORE creation (Lucifer fell before Eden).
Verse 12:10-11 - Victory Through the Lamb
"Now is come salvation, and strength, and the kingdom of our God, and the power of his Christ:
for the accuser of our brethren is cast down, which accused them before our God day and night.
And they overcame him by the blood of the Lamb, and by the word of their testimony; and they
loved not their lives unto the death."
HOW Satan is overcome: 1. Blood of the Lamb - Jesus' sacrifice 2. Word of their testimony -
Faithful witness 3. Loved not their lives unto death - Willing to die for truth
Verse 12:12 - Satan's Short Time
"Woe to the inhabiters of the earth and of the sea! for the devil is come down unto you, having
great wrath, because he knoweth that he hath but a short time."


---

Satan knows his time is SHORT. This is why evil is intensifying.
APPLICATION TO 2026: Satan knows the fig tree generation (1948 + 70-80 years) is almost
complete. He knows time is running out. This explains the exponential increase in: - Deception - Moral
decay - Violence - Attacks on God's commandments - Push toward global government and religion
Verse 12:13-16 - Persecution and Protection
"And when the dragon saw that he was cast unto the earth, he persecuted the woman which
brought forth the man child. And to the woman were given two wings of a great eagle, that she
might fly into the wilderness, into her place, where she is nourished for a time, and times, and
half a time, from the face of the serpent."
The same 1,260-year period (time, times, and half a time).
"Two wings of a great eagle" - God's protection and deliverance (Exodus 19:4, Deuteronomy
32:11-12)
Verse 15-16: Satan tried to destroy the faithful through persecution ("flood" of armies), but God
protected them ("earth helped the woman").
Verse 12:17 - THE REMNANT (God's People in 2026)
"And the dragon was wroth with the woman, and went to make war with the remnant of her
seed, which keep the commandments of God, and have the testimony of Jesus Christ."
THIS IS THE KEY VERSE FOR 2026.
After the 1,260 years ended (1798), Satan goes after the REMNANT - the final generation.

The remnant has: - The commandments of God (including Sabbath) - The spirit of prophecy (prophetic
gift/understanding)

(commandments).
