Chapter 10: Revelation 13 - The Two Beasts and the Mark
This is the MOST CRITICAL chapter for understanding 2026.
THE FIRST BEAST - Rising From the Sea (Revelation 13:1-10)
Verse 13:1: "And I stood upon the sand of the sea, and saw a beast rise up out of the sea, having seven
heads and ten horns, and upon his horns ten crowns, and upon his heads the name of blasphemy."
BIBLICAL DEFINITIONS: - Beast = Kingdom/political power (Daniel 7:17, 23) - Sea = Peoples,
multitudes, nations (Revelation 17:15) - Heads = Mountains/kingdoms (Revelation 17:9) - Horns =
Kings/kingdoms (Daniel 7:24, Revelation 17:12)
This beast rises from densely populated Europe.
Verse 13:2: "And the beast which I saw was like unto a leopard, and his feet were as the feet of a bear,
and his mouth as the mouth of a lion: and the dragon gave him his power, and his seat, and great
authority."
COMPOSITE BEAST - Contains characteristics of ALL Daniel's beasts: - Leopard body = Greece
(Daniel 7:6) - Bear feet = Medo-Persia (Daniel 7:5) - Lion mouth = Babylon (Daniel 7:4)
This is Rome (Papal Rome) carrying forward the characteristics of all previous kingdoms.
"Dragon gave him his power, seat, and authority" - Satan gave the Papacy: 1. Power 2. Seat (throne
- when Constantine moved to Constantinople, he left Rome to the Bishops) 3. Authority
HISTORICAL FACT: Emperor Constantine transferred the capital from Rome to Constantinople
(330 AD), leaving Rome to the Popes. The Papacy inherited the seat of the Roman Empire.
The Identifying Characteristics of the First Beast
1. NAME OF BLASPHEMY (Verse 1)
What is blasphemy?
John 10:33: "For a good work we stone thee not; but for blasphemy; and because that thou, being a
man, makest thyself God."
Mark 2:7: "Why doth this man thus speak blasphemies? who can forgive sins but God only?"
Blasphemy = (a) Man claiming to be God, (b) Man claiming to forgive sins
PAPAL CLAIMS: - Pope's titles: "Holy Father" (John 17:11 - reserved for God), "Vicar of Christ"
(substitute for Christ), "Vicar of the Son of God" - Claims to forgive sins: The confessional system
claims priests can forgive sins - Papal infallibility: When speaking ex cathedra, the Pope cannot err


---

These are blasphemous claims.
2. POWER FOR 42 MONTHS (Verse 5)
"And there was given unto him a mouth speaking great things and blasphemies; and power was
given unto him to continue forty and two months."
42 months = 42 × 30 days = 1,260 days = 1,260 YEARS (day-year principle)
FULFILLMENT: 538 AD - 1798 AD
- 538 AD: Last opposing kingdom (Ostrogoths) destroyed; Papal supremacy begins - 1798 AD:
Napoleon's general Berthier takes Pope Pius VI captive; papal power broken
EXACT 1,260 YEARS
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED - but the wound is healing (verse 3)
3. MAKES WAR WITH THE SAINTS (Verse 7)
"And it was given unto him to make war with the saints, and to overcome them."
FULFILLMENT: The Dark Ages - Inquisition, torture, burning at the stake: - Waldenses massacred -
Albigenses destroyed - Huguenots killed (St. Bartholomew's Day Massacre - 70,000 in one night) -
Anyone with a Bible in their own language executed - Conservative estimates: 50-150 million martyrs
STATUS IN 2026: FULFILLED historically - but Revelation 13:15 indicates persecution will come
again
4. DEADLY WOUND (Verse 3)
"And I saw one of his heads as it were wounded to death; and his deadly wound was healed: and
all the world wondered after the beast."
DEADLY WOUND: 1798 AD - Pope taken captive, dies in exile, temporal power lost
WOUND BEGINS HEALING: 1929 - Lateran Treaty signed, Vatican becomes independent state
WOUND FULLY HEALED - APPLICATION TO 2026: - Pope meets with world leaders as equal
head of state - Pope addresses United Nations - Pope influences global policy - World leaders visit
Vatican - Pope Leo XIV (2025) - "The Lion" speaks with authority - "All the world wondered after the
beast" - FULFILLED NOW
The Papacy has regained its influence. The world is wondering (following with admiration).
5. SITS ON SEVEN MOUNTAINS (Revelation 17:9)


---

"The seven heads are seven mountains, on which the woman sitteth."
Rome has been called "the city on seven hills" throughout history: 1. Capitoline 2. Palatine 3. Aventine
4. Caelian 5. Esquiline 6. Viminal 7. Quirinal
FULFILLMENT: Undisputed - Rome sits on seven hills
THE SECOND BEAST - Rising From the Earth (Revelation 13:11-18)
Verse 13:11: "And I beheld another beast coming up out of the earth; and he had two horns like a
lamb, and he spake as a dragon."
CONTRASTS WITH FIRST BEAST: First Beast | Second Beast
Rises from SEA (populated Europe) | Rises from EARTH (sparsely populated area) Has 7 heads, 10
horns (many kingdoms) | Has 2 horns (two principles of power) Blasphemous names | Lamb-like
(Christ-like principles) Given power by dragon | Speaks AS dragon (eventually) Rose around 538 AD |
Rises around 1798 AD (when first beast wounded)
IDENTIFICATION: When the first beast received its deadly wound (1798), what nation was rising to
power in a sparsely populated territory with lamb-like (Christ-like, freedom-based) principles?
THE UNITED STATES OF AMERICA
TWO HORNS LIKE A LAMB: Horns = power. Lamb = Christ-like principles.
America's two founding principles: 1. Republicanism - Civil liberty, no king ("We the People") 2.
Protestantism - Religious liberty, no pope (First Amendment - "Congress shall make no law respecting
an establishment of religion")
These were LAMB-LIKE - freedom, liberty, separation of church and state.
"SPEAKS AS A DRAGON":
A nation "speaks" through its laws and policies.
PROPHECY: America, which began with religious freedom, will eventually speak like Satan - using
force in matters of religion.
STATUS IN 2026: This transformation is BEGINNING NOW.
What the Second Beast Does
Verse 13:12: "And he exerciseth all the power of the first beast before him, and causeth the earth and
them which dwell therein to worship the first beast, whose deadly wound was healed."


---

PROPHECY: 1. USA will exercise the SAME KIND of power as the Papacy (religious persecution
through civil authority) 2. USA will CAUSE the world to worship (follow/submit to) the first beast
(Papacy)
APPLICATION TO 2026 - BEGINNING: - Religious Right gaining political power in USA -
Christian Nationalism movement growing - Sunday law proposals being discussed - USA still has
global influence to pressure other nations - Calls for "return to Christian values" (but man's tradition,
not God's commandments)
Verse 13:13-14: "And he doeth great wonders, so that he maketh fire come down from heaven on the
earth in the sight of men, And deceiveth them that dwell on the earth by the means of those miracles."
MIRACLES/WONDERS: This could be: - Literal miraculous signs (2 Thessalonians 2:9 - "lying
wonders") - Technological "wonders" that seem miraculous - Spiritual manifestations through
charismatic movements
APPLICATION TO 2026: - Signs and wonders movement in Christianity - Technology that seems
like "magic" (AI, holograms, deepfakes) - Possible demonic manifestations disguised as "moves of
God"
2 Thessalonians 2:9-10: "Even him, whose coming is after the working of Satan with all power and
signs and lying wonders, And with all deceivableness of unrighteousness in them that perish; because
they received not the love of the truth."
THE IMAGE TO THE BEAST (Verses 13:14-15)
"Saying to them that dwell on the earth, that they should make an image to the beast, which had
the wound by a sword, and did live. And he had power to give life unto the image of the beast,
that the image of the beast should both speak, and cause that as many as would not worship the
image of the beast should be killed."
WHAT IS AN IMAGE?
An image is a copy or likeness.
What was the beast's system? - Union of church and state - Religious laws enforced by civil power -
Persecution of dissenters
The image to the beast = America creating the SAME system: - Union of church and state - Religious
laws (Sunday laws) enforced by government - Persecution of those who refuse
"GIVE LIFE UNTO THE IMAGE":
Greek word for "life" = pneuma = breath/spirit


---

Genesis 2:7: "And the LORD God formed man of the dust of the ground, and breathed into his nostrils
the breath of life; and man became a living soul."
When God breathed into man, man could SPEAK.
The image is given "breath" so it can SPEAK.
APPLICATION TO 2026 - ARTIFICIAL INTELLIGENCE:
AI has been given "breath" (animation/life): - AI can SPEAK (ChatGPT, Claude, voice AI) - AI can
make decisions - AI can control systems - AI can identify individuals (facial recognition) - AI can
enforce economic sanctions (digital currency) - AI is being developed primarily in USA (Silicon Valley
- Google, Microsoft, OpenAI, Anthropic)
The second beast (USA) is literally giving "breath" to the image (technology) so it can "speak"
(communicate and command).
"Cause that as many as would not worship the image...should be killed":
Economic death first (can't buy or sell - verse 17), then physical death threats.
This hasn't been FULLY implemented yet, but the TECHNOLOGY exists NOW.
THE MARK OF THE BEAST (Verses 13:16-18)
"And he causeth all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and bond, to receive a mark in
their right hand, or in their foreheads: And that no man might buy or sell, save he that had the
mark, or the name of the beast, or the number of his name."
WHO ENFORCES THE MARK? The second beast (USA) - verse 16 says "HE causeth all"
WHERE IS THE MARK RECEIVED? - Forehead = Mind/belief/decision (you believe it's right) -
Right hand = Actions/work (you comply to survive)
WHAT IS THE MARK?
The mark is the OPPOSITE of God's seal.
GOD'S SEAL (Ezekiel 20:12, 20): - The seventh-day Sabbath (Saturday) - Sign of God as Creator -
Sign of God's authority
THE BEAST'S MARK (Catholic Church's own admission):
"Sunday is our mark of authority... The church is above the Bible, and this transference of
Sabbath observance is proof of that fact." - Catholic Record, September 1, 1923


---

"Of course the Catholic Church claims that the change was her act... And the act is a mark of her
ecclesiastical power." - H.F. Thomas, Chancellor of Cardinal Gibbons
The Papacy ITSELF identifies Sunday observance as its mark of authority - the change from God's
Sabbath (seventh day/Saturday) to Sunday (first day).
When Does It Become the Mark?
Simply going to church on Sunday NOW is not the mark. The mark is received when: 1. The issue is
clearly presented (Sabbath vs. Sunday) 2. A person understands the truth 3. Sunday worship is
ENFORCED BY LAW 4. A person chooses to obey man's law rather than God's commandment
APPLICATION TO 2026 - BUILDING TOWARD ENFORCEMENT:
The infrastructure is being built: - Digital currency systems (control buying/selling) - Social credit
scores (China model, spreading globally) - Vaccine passports (precedent for digital ID tied to
compliance) - Facial recognition (identify non-compliers) - AI enforcement systems - Sunday law
proposals (being discussed in religious-right circles)
Climate change will likely be the excuse: - "We need a day of rest for the planet" - "Sunday as
universal rest day will reduce carbon emissions" - "Climate crisis requires everyone to comply"
NONE of this is the mark YET. But the pieces are being positioned.
666 - THE NUMBER OF THE BEAST (Verse 13:18)
"Here is wisdom. Let him that hath understanding count the number of the beast: for it is the
number of a man; and his number is Six hundred threescore and six."
"The number of A man" - not mankind in general, but a specific man/system.
6 = MAN'S NUMBER: - Man created on day 6 (Genesis 1:26-31) - 6 is one short of 7 (God's number
of perfection) - 6 represents human effort, human system, man apart from God
666 = TRIPLE 6: - Complete human system - Man attempting to be God - Complete rebellion
666 represents: 1. Man's day instead of God's day (Sunday instead of Sabbath) 2. Man's law instead
of God's law (human tradition instead of commandments) 3. Man claiming to be God (Pope claiming
God's titles and authority)
2 Thessalonians 2:3-4: "That man of sin be revealed, the son of perdition; Who opposeth and exalteth
himself above all that is called God, or that is worshipped; so that he as God sitteth in the temple of
God, shewing himself that he is God."

MAN SAYS: We changed it to the first day (Sunday)

THE FIRST ANGEL (Verses 14:6-7)
"And I saw another angel fly in the midst of heaven, having the everlasting gospel to preach unto
them that dwell on the earth, and to every nation, and kindred, and tongue, and people, Saying
with a loud voice, Fear God, and give glory to him; for the hour of his judgment is come: and
worship him that made heaven, and earth, and the sea, and the fountains of waters."
KEY ELEMENTS:
1. Everlasting gospel - Salvation through Jesus Christ alone 2. To every nation - Worldwide
proclamation 3. Fear God, give glory - Reverence and obedience 4. Hour of judgment is come - We
are in the judgment NOW 5. Worship the Creator - "made heaven, and earth, and the sea, and
fountains"
THIS IS A DIRECT QUOTE FROM THE FOURTH COMMANDMENT:
Exodus 20:11: "For in six days the LORD made heaven and earth, the sea, and all that in them is, and
rested the seventh day: wherefore the LORD blessed the sabbath day, and hallowed it."
The first angel calls the world back to: - Worship the Creator (not the beast) - Keep God's
commandments (including the Sabbath) - Recognize we're in the judgment
APPLICATION TO 2026: The first angel's message IS going forth - calling people back to true
worship of the Creator and keeping God's commandments (including Sabbath).
THE SECOND ANGEL (Verse 14:8)
"And there followed another angel, saying, Babylon is fallen, is fallen, that great city, because she
made all nations drink of the wine of the wrath of her fornication."
BABYLON = The fallen religious system (Papacy and apostate churches)

THE THIRD ANGEL (Verses 14:9-12)

1. INTERPRETIVE FRAMEWORK


---

Historicist/Adventist Hermeneutic
This analysis follows the historicist method of prophetic interpretation, which understands Bible
prophecy as unfolding progressively through history from the time of the prophet to the end of time.
This is in contrast to preterism (all fulfilled in the past) or futurism (all to be fulfilled in a brief future
period).
Core principle: Let the Bible interpret itself.
"To the law and to the testimony: if they speak not according to this word, it is because there is no light
in them." — Isaiah 8:20
Spiritual Israel — The True Israel of God
A critical foundation for understanding end-time prophecy is recognizing that "Israel" in the New
Testament context refers to spiritual Israel — those who are in Christ by faith — not the modern
nation-state established in 1948.
Scripture Foundation
Romans 9:6-8 — "Not as though the word of God hath taken none effect. For they are not all Israel,
which are of Israel: Neither, because they are the seed of Abraham, are they all children: but, In Isaac
shall thy seed be called. That is, They which are the children of the flesh, these are not the children
of God: but the children of the promise are counted for the seed."
Galatians 3:7, 29 — "Know ye therefore that they which are of faith, the same are the children of
Abraham... And if ye be Christ's, then are ye Abraham's seed, and heirs according to the promise."
Romans 2:28-29 — "For he is not a Jew, which is one outwardly; neither is that circumcision, which
is outward in the flesh: But he is a Jew, which is one inwardly; and circumcision is that of the heart, in
the spirit, and not in the letter; whose praise is not of men, but of God."
Galatians 6:16 — "And as many as walk according to this rule, peace be on them, and mercy, and
upon the Israel of God."
Two Jerusalems

1984 — The Wound Begins to Heal
On May 2, 1984, President Ronald Reagan met Pope John Paul II in Fairbanks, Alaska — the first
meeting between a U.S. President and Pope on American soil after the establishment of formal
diplomatic relations.
Reagan stated: "For over a century, we maintained warm and fruitful, but informal relations. Now we
have exchanged ambassadors."
UPI Archives (May 2, 1984): "It was the first time that the two leaders have met since the United
States established diplomatic relations with the Vatican in January, and the first time ever on American
soil."

influence in American and global affairs.

beast should both speak, and cause that as many as would not worship the image of the beast should

The image SPEAKS — it issues commands, renders judgments, makes declarations.
The image CAUSES — it enforces, compels, executes.
AI does both: - AI speaks: "Non-compliant. Benefits terminated. Employment flagged. Tracking
initiated." - AI causes: Automated enforcement. No human override. No appeal. No mercy.
13. BIBLICAL DEFINITION OF "SPEAK"
Let the Bible Define Itself
When a nation or power "speaks" in Scripture, it legislates, decrees, commands.
Daniel 3 — Nebuchadnezzar's Image
Daniel 3:4-6 — "Then an herald cried aloud, To you it is commanded, O people, nations, and
languages, That at what time ye hear the sound of the cornet, flute, harp, sackbut, psaltery, dulcimer,
and all kinds of musick, ye fall down and worship the golden image that Nebuchadnezzar the king hath
set up: And whoso falleth not down and worshippeth shall the same hour be cast into the midst of a
burning fiery furnace."
When Babylon spoke — it decreed worship with death penalty for non-compliance.


---

Daniel 6 — Darius's Decree
Daniel 6:7-9 — "All the presidents of the kingdom, the governors, and the princes, the counsellors, and
the captains, have consulted together to establish a royal statute, and to make a firm decree, that
whosoever shall ask a petition of any God or man for thirty days, save of thee, O king, he shall be cast
into the den of lions... Wherefore king Darius signed the writing and the decree."
When Medo-Persia spoke — it legislated worship with death penalty.
Application to Revelation 13:11
Revelation 13:11 — "And I beheld another beast coming up out of the earth; and he had two horns like
a lamb, and he spake as a dragon."
To speak = to legislate. To decree. To command.
When America "speaks as a dragon," it's not just words — it's LAWS.
Application to Revelation 13:15
Revelation 13:15 — "And he had power to give life unto the image of the beast, that the image of the
beast should both SPEAK, and CAUSE..."
The image SPEAKS = The image LEGISLATES.
The image CAUSES = The image ENFORCES.
The United States Is Speaking Right Now
Every executive order, every task force, every piece of legislation — that's the beast speaking.
And it's speaking as a dragon — coercion, control, persecution.
Wrapped in lamb's clothing — "fraud prevention," "election integrity," "religious liberty,"
"rededication to God."
But the speech is dragon speech. The laws are dragon laws.
