Revelation 12:1-2 - The Woman and the Dragon:
"And there appeared a great wonder in heaven; a woman clothed with the sun, and the moon under her
feet, and upon her head a crown of twelve stars: And she being with child cried, travailing in birth, and
pained to be delivered."
And there appeared another wonder in heaven; and behold a great red dragon, having seven
heads and ten horns, and seven crowns upon his heads.
Scripture's Definition: - The Woman = The church, God's people, Israel (symbolism of 12 tribes/12
apostles) - Clothed with the sun = Clothed with Christ's righteousness - Moon under feet = Standing
above earthly powers - Crown of twelve stars = The 12 tribes/apostles - Travailing in birth = The
END TIMES labor pains (referenced by Paul in 1 Thess 5:3) - The Dragon = Satan himself
(Revelation 12:9) - Seven heads and ten horns = The beast system
Revelation 13: The Two Beasts
Revelation 13:1-7 - The First Beast (Papal Rome):
"And I stood upon the sand of the sea, and saw a beast rise up out of the sea, having seven heads and
ten horns, and upon his horns ten crowns, and upon his heads the name of blasphemy... And the dragon
gave him his power, and his seat, and great authority... And power was given unto him to continue forty
and two months."
Identifying Characteristics: - Seven heads and ten horns = The kingdoms and rulers of the earth -
Names of blasphemy = Claims that belong to God alone - Dragon gave him power = Satanic
authorization - 42 months = 1,260 days = 1,260 years of dominance
Scripture's Definition of Blasphemy: Making claims that only God can make. The Papal system
claims: - Authority to forgive sins (only Christ) - Infallibility (only God) - Ability to grant salvation
(only Christ)
Revelation 13:7-10 - The Beast Makes War on Saints:
"And it was given unto him to make war with the saints, and to overcome them: and power was given
him over all kindreds, and tongues, and nations. And all that dwell upon the earth shall worship him,
whose names are not written in the book of life of the Lamb slain from the foundation of the world."
Definition: The beast system: - Makes WAR with the saints (believers) - Overcomes many of them -
Has power over all nations - Demands worship from all except the faithful
Revelation 13:11-17 - The Second Beast (The United States)
Revelation 13:11-12 - The Second Beast Emerges:


---

"And I beheld another beast coming up out of the earth; and he had two horns like a lamb, and he spake
as a dragon... And he exerciseth all the power of the first beast before him, and causeth the earth and
which dwell therein to worship the first beast."
Scripture's Definition: - Comes up out of the earth = Emerges from the new world (not the

Revelation 13:13-14 - Deceptive Signs and Wonders:
"And he doeth great wonders, so that he maketh fire come down from heaven on the earth in the sight

the beast."
Definition: The second beast: - Performs MIRACLES and signs - Uses these to DECEIVE people -

The IMAGE OF THE BEAST = A representation or system through which people worship the beast.

Revelation 13:15-17 - The Mark of the Beast
Revelation 13:15-16 - The Command to Worship:
"And he had power to give life unto the image of the beast, that the image of the beast should both
speak, and cause that as many as would not worship the image of the beast should be killed. And he

Scripture's Definition: - The image speaks (can communicate, give commands) - Those who refuse to

This is ABSOLUTE CONTROL. No one can purchase food, shelter, medicine, or any necessity

Revelation 14: The Three Angels' Messages - God's Final Warning
Revelation 14:6-7 - First Angel's Message (The Everlasting Gospel):
"And I saw another angel fly in the midst of heaven, having the everlasting gospel to preach unto them

voice, Fear God, and give glory to him; for the hour of his judgment is come: and worship him that

Scripture's Message: - Fear God (reverence Him above all) - Give glory to Him (worship Him

Revelation 14:8 - Second Angel's Message (Babylon Has Fallen):

Revelation 14:9-11 - Third Angel's Message (The Warning About the Mark):

tormented with fire and brimstone in the presence of the holy angels, and in the presence of the Lamb:

Revelation 15-16: The Seven Vials of God's Wrath
Revelation 15:1 - God's Complete Judgment:

The first five vials bring: 1. Grievous sores upon those with the mark (16:2) 2. Sea becomes blood -

Definition: The final gathering of all nations for judgment.
Revelation 16:17-21 - The Seventh Vial - It Is Done:

Revelation 17-18: The Fall of Babylon
Revelation 17:1-5 - The Harlot Described:
"And there came one of the seven angels which had the seven vials, and talked with me, saying unto

---

So he carried me away in the spirit into the wilderness: and I saw a woman sit upon a scarlet coloured
beast, full of names of blasphemy... And upon her forehead was a name written, MYSTERY,

EARTH."
Scripture's Definition of Babylon: - A harlot = Unfaithful to God, fornicating with nations - Sitteth

Revelation 17:15-17 - The Harlot's Identity:
"And he saith unto me, The waters which thou sawest, where the whore sitteth, are peoples, and

purpose.
Revelation 18:1-8 - Babylon Falls:
"And after these things I saw another angel come down from heaven, having great power; and the earth

and them that worshipped his image. These both were cast alive into a lake of fire burning with

Revelation 21-22: The New Heaven and Earth
Revelation 21:1-4 - God's Eternal Home With His People:

Revelation 22:14-15 - Who Enters:

TRIGGERS THE NEXT
The Trigger Chain
1. ISRAEL BECOMES A NATION (1948) - Fulfills the fig tree parable - Starts the 70-80 year
generation count - Sets the prophetic clock ticking
2. THE PEACE AND SAFETY DECLARATION (2026) - The Board of Peace established - Pope
invited to join global governance - World declaring "peace" - This is 1 Thessalonians 5:3 fulfilled
3. SUDDEN DESTRUCTION FOLLOWS (IMMINENT) - The mark system is implemented -
Economic control mechanisms activate - Persecution of believers begins - The abomination of
desolation is set up
4. THE MARK SYSTEM ENFORCED - No one can buy or sell without it - Sunday Sabbath worship
is required - Those who refuse face persecution and death - The faithful are tested
5. GOD'S JUDGMENTS BEGIN (THE SEALS, TRUMPETS, AND VIALS) - The earth shakes
with earthquakes - Plagues afflict those with the mark - The heavens are darkened - Chaos engulfs the

PLAIN LANGUAGE SUMMARY: WHAT THIS ALL MEANS
In the simplest terms, what we are seeing is the assembly of a Global Digital Cage.
If you strip away the complex laws and the prophetic language, it means that the world is moving from
a system of "Inherent Rights" to a system of "Conditional Permissions."
Here is what that looks like for the average person:
1. Your Identity is Now Your "Key"
Instead of just being "you," your ability to function in society is being tied to a digital profile
anchored to your body (biometrics like your face, eyes, or fingerprints). This profile is checked by a
computer every 30 days.
2. The "Monthly Pulse"


---

Think of it like a subscription to your own life. Every month, the government "washes" its databases.
If there is a typo in your file, an issue with your name, or a "flag" on your status, the computer
automatically turns off your "key."
Because this is handled by AI and strict laws, a human clerk can't just "fix it" for you — the system
has no mercy.
3. The "Energy Veto" (The Power Switch)
To make sure everyone uses this digital key, the government is taking control of the world's "gas tank"
(the oil and gas in places like Venezuela and the Middle East).
- If a business or a person isn't "compliant" with the new digital standards, the system can simply
"unplug" them. - No energy means no credit card processing, no gas for your car, and no electricity
for your home. - It is a way to force everyone into the system without needing to use physical force.
4. The Biblical "Big Picture"
In the Bible, this is exactly what is described in the book of Revelation: a system where you cannot
"buy or sell" unless you are part of a specific, government-mandated identification loop.
- The "Lamb" (America's promise of freedom) is now using the "Voice of the Dragon" (forceful laws
and military power) to make this happen. - We are currently in the "Construction Phase" (2026). -
The "Lock-and-Key Phase" (where the gates fully close) is what the timeline suggests is coming by
2027.
THE BOTTOM LINE
It means that very soon, everything — your job, your food, your bank account, and your legal
status — will depend on a single digital green light that must be refreshed every 30 days.
If that light turns red, the system is designed to "veto" your participation in the world until you
comply with its requirements.
It is the transition from being a free citizen to being an "administered subject" in a global database.
